Locarno Issue: Britain, France, and Belgium Issue Declarations; Meeting to be Held in London Tomorrow; Plans to Solve Problems Comprehensively; Achieve Consolidation of European Peace 32

(Paris) Regarding the Locarno Conference, the governments of Britain, France, and Belgium recently issued a public announcement at 2:40 this afternoon in their respective capitals, stating: "The representatives of Britain, France, and Belgium held the first Locarno Conference in London on March 19 and established a draft agreement. Now, after exchanging opinions, it has been decided to hold another meeting in London on the 23rd of this month to discuss the current international situation and to consider what appropriate methods should be used to realize the aspirations of each country to comprehensively solve problems and consolidate peace." (21st, Havas News Agency dispatch)

(London) Regarding the Locarno Conference, the French Ambassador, Gorpine, recently visited Foreign Secretary Eden again this morning and agreed to publish the first joint declaration of Britain, France, and Belgium before the meeting, in accordance with the suggestions made by France. The second declaration will only be issued after the meeting. The British government also requested the French government to undertake the drafting work to limit the scope of the three-nation conference and stated that this meeting is of a preparatory nature. Once it is over, a five-nation conference should be convened so that Germany and Italy can come out and participate. (21st, Havas dispatch)

(London) The highest British diplomatic authority recently issued a declaration to the press in the afternoon, roughly saying that the three-nation conference of Britain, France, and Belgium must avoid discussing various issues related to general policies and focus on preparing for the five-nation conference as its main purpose. The initiators of recent diplomatic problems have been countries promoting dictatorial systems, while democratic countries have mostly followed behind. The convening of this three-nation conference allows democratic countries to take diplomatic initiative again and restore their original position. After the three-nation conference is held, the five-nation conference will be convened, with Italy and Germany participating, and then a broader European conference will be convened. As far as the five-nation conference is concerned, its main purpose is to conclude a new Western European convention to replace the Locarno Convention. In addition, the issue of resolving the general situation in Europe should also be mentioned. The location of the last Great War was not in Western Europe. If you want to appease the situation, the various problems in other parts of Europe should also be discussed. In the current state of Europe, democratic countries and dictatorial countries will be divided into two major groups, confronting each other. In the eyes of the British government, this trend should be avoided by the five-nation conference. According to what our reporter knows, the British government wants to strictly limit the scope of discussion of the three-nation conference to avoid causing a backlash from Italy and Germany. However, the three-nation conference will definitely be held as scheduled. Even if Italy and Germany have criticisms, they are not acceptable to Britain. (21st, Havas dispatch)

Where is the Hirota Cabinet Going? (4) 33

— Jia He

Prime Minister Hirota's response to this "historical speech" is "establishing constitutional government", and what about Army Minister Terauchi? He publicly announced to Saito: "I have the same feelings about the purpose of the speech. From now on, active-duty soldiers will participate in politics, and I, an unworthy person, will carry it out." People generally believe that Saito's speech was only a verbal victory, which is quite a misunderstanding. The mission of the Hirota Cabinet is not to use high-pressure means to subdue the military, but to have the power to put the military slightly on the right track. Because his regime is transitional. During the transition period, he suppresses leftists and corrects rightists. From a historical point of view, the rise of the military is by no means the personal will of Baron Araki and General Masaki. Instead, there is an undeniable trend behind him, that is, the crisis of Japanese capitalism after the Wakatsuki Cabinet and weak diplomacy. At present, the London Treaty, which the young officers consider a great shame, has become waste paper, and the continental policy they hold is being completed one by one; moreover, the unexpected victory over China and the development of Manchuria have not only temporarily alleviated the crisis of Japanese capitalism, but even the petty bourgeoisie, who have always been dissatisfied with the regime, have lost their enthusiasm for supporting radical fascism. Unless the proletarian movement stimulates it; unless the equilibrium point on which the Hirota Cabinet stands is broken, it is very difficult for radical fascism to take the stage at present. For the above reasons, the military during the Hirota Cabinet era took the Terauchi type, not the Araki type. When General Araki was rampant, the actors of the "May 15th" incident were not only at large, but also carried the crown of protecting the imperial country; during General Terauchi's tenure, the coup leaders of the "February 26th" incident were not only severely punished, but also engraved on their foreheads with the crime of traitors. These distinctions can be proved by the military court authorities' announcement of Lieutenant Colonel Aizawa's death sentence the day after Saito's speech (May 9). At this time, Manui, who defended Aizawa, was demoted to a member of the General Staff Headquarters, and Dr. Uzawa had already disappeared.

The temporary retreat of the military is also the demise of a certain group of political parties. Here we should point out to the reader Fusanosuke Kuhara. This loyal supporter of General Yoshikazu Tanaka, a politician of the Japanese industrial chaebol, is the person whom Takao Saito called linked to the military. Before the coup, with a single effort, he gained three million yen from the stock market. After the coup, suddenly newspapers and publications called him "missing". It is said that a prominent radical fascist politician would be "missing" in the "China bandit country" (Dalian Mitsui's description of our country), but in a country that claims to be a defender of East Asian civilization, it would simply become incredible. However, the Shanghai Japanese Daily News published a piece of news at that time that Kuhara was imprisoned with more than seventy members of parliament who were bribed. If it was only for this sesame-like matter that he was imprisoned, he would never be "missing". Moreover, the situation that "re-emergence is probably impossible" can be expected to be very serious. His demise meant that the Seiyukai lost a director who was good at making trouble; on the political stage, there was a lack of a strong general who would stir up trouble with Araki and others from time to time. However, this can only be regarded as the demise of the "National Polity Clarification Faction", and cannot be regarded as the demise of the chaebol he represents. Not to mention that all the shares owned by Kuhara were taken over by the Nomura chaebol, and Nissan, which was controlled by Yoshisuke Aikawa, was still thriving with the support of the military's "national automobile policy." Why is this so? Originally, Kuhara's activities, in addition to seeking benefits for the Nissan chaebol, also mixed personal motives. He wanted to overthrow President Suzuki and did not hesitate to create factions within the Seiyukai; he wanted to collude with Araki to seize power and raised the banner against the group of senior officials, even to the point where he, as a "constitutional politician", joined hands with the young officers who took direct action; these were personal behaviors and had little to do with Nissan. But from another perspective, the development of Nissan chaebol's military industry cannot lack the military, and the people who are responsible for communication are the Kuhara. Now that Kuhara has fallen due to personal motives and behaviors, Nissan chaebol's military industry is still expanding to meet the needs of Japanese capitalism at this stage.

Page 8

Turkish Government Dispatches Troops into the Straits Zone; Demilitarized Zone Abolished; National Flag Raised in Celebration; Montreux Convention Signed, a Major Event After the European War 34

Istanbul, Turkey – The new Straits Convention was officially signed in Montreux today. The Turkish government ordered General İsmet İnönü, the Prime Minister, to personally lead troops and enter the Straits zone at midnight to garrison. The demilitarized zone of the Dardanelles Strait after the European War has been abolished. The Turkish government, in celebration of the restoration of sovereignty, has designated this day as a national day of celebration. (20th National Telegram)

The Capital of Turkey – According to the new Straits Convention, Turkey can immediately re-establish fortifications in the Dardanelles and Bosphorus Straits. A large contingent of the country's army formally entered the Straits zone last night. Flags were raised everywhere this morning to mark the celebration. Loudspeakers were installed everywhere to broadcast the Montreux Conference’s signing of the new convention and various patriotic songs. A torchlight parade was held in the capital last night, with soldiers and the public participating. They circled once in front of the statue of President Kemal Atatürk and were reviewed by government officials in front of the Ministry of National Defense. Istanbul, being within the demilitarized zone, had all its streets with flags flying and electric lights illuminating as if it were daytime. The public cheered as the troops passed by. Several warships, adorned with lanterns, slowly entered the Bosphorus Strait, followed by many small boats, to show that under the leadership of President Kemal Atatürk, Turkey has restored sovereignty over the two straits. The local residents cheered thunderously, marking a grand occasion. (21st Havas Telegram)

Montreux – The Montreux Conference held its final meeting tonight at 10:15 PM for the signing ceremony of the new Straits Convention and adjourned at 11:00 PM. From its opening on the 22nd of last month, excluding a ten-day recess in the middle, it lasted a total of nineteen days before coming to a conclusion. At tonight's meeting, representatives from each country signed the treaty in turn, followed by the Turkish chief representative, Foreign Minister Rüşdü, who delivered a speech saying, "For those countries that have not sent representatives to participate in today's conference, I hope that they will either sign and join directly in the future, or provide moral support for the new convention signed today." After his speech, Lord Stanley, the British representative, Mr. Litvinov, the Soviet representative, and Mr. Titulescu, the Romanian representative, successively spoke, all stating that the results of this conference were extremely important. The Japanese representative, Mr. Sato, also rose to speak, saying, "Japan is currently not a member state of the League of Nations, which is where our difficulty lies. In this situation, we cannot but raise reservations about certain points of the new convention. However, apart from this, our government will fully respect the provisions and spirit of this convention and provide convenience for its implementation. The measures established by the Montreux Conference aim to safeguard peace in the Near East, and its positive impact may also extend to the distant Asian continent. This is what I sincerely pray for." Then, representatives from other countries, including the French representative Mr. Boncour, also spoke, and the meeting was then declared adjourned. (20th Havas Agency Telegram)

Montreux – After the signing of the new Dardanelles and Bosphorus Straits Convention, political figures have all attached great importance to it, saying that it is the first time that one of the peace treaties of the European War has been amended through legal means. It is also the first time that Japan has signed an international treaty after withdrawing from the League of Nations. It is also said that although Italy did not participate in the Montreux Conference, it will contact Turkey directly as soon as possible to join the new convention. Both Turkey and the Soviet Russia, which are most concerned about the new Straits system, have felt satisfied. According to news from Turkey, the government and the public have celebrated the restoration of the right to arm the straits and the restoration of complete sovereignty over part of their territory. The situation is very enthusiastic. As for Soviet Russia, the benefits it can obtain according to the new convention are even greater than those it had during the Tsarist era. If war breaks out in the future, it can both block the Black Sea and control it, and its fleet can freely enter and exit the Black Sea. Although other countries have made many concessions on this level, the main interests of these countries are not in danger as a result. In short, the sincere cooperation of the countries in the Black Sea region has been fully realized due to the establishment of the new convention. This is something that all the delegations are happy about. (21st Havas Agency Telegram)

Can Return to China After February

British House of Lords Discusses Far East Issues; Smuggling in North China Harms All Countries; British Embassy in Peiping Does Not Give Up; British-Japanese Relations Have Not Reached a Compromise 36

(London) The House of Lords debated the smuggling situation in North China today. Opposition leader Lord Marley criticized the attitude of British merchants in Shanghai, saying that they cannot entirely blame the Japanese for the decline of British trade in China due to illegal and unfair competition; British merchants in Shanghai must also bear some responsibility. This difficulty may be resolved by the League of Nations. If Japanese aggression against China continues unabated, China will inevitably rely on Russian friendship to resist Japan. Marley then cited a recent satirical cartoon in the Shanghai North-China Daily News, depicting China connecting a telephone between Tokyo and Berlin. Locals in Shanghai believe that the Japanese occupation of the Municipal Council is commonplace, and many Britons also think so.

Today's debate was initiated by former Secretary of State for India, Lord Peel, who said that the situation in North China now needs constant attention. He then elaborated on the smuggling situation there, saying that recently two batches of bullets and armaments have been transported, and those who sell drugs will of course take this opportunity to pour drugs into China. A significant number of these goods are manufactured in Japan and can now be transported at will. The impact on China's finances can be easily foreseen. It should be known that this not only disrupts China's trade but also hinders China's foreign debt secured by tariffs. It is conceivable what kind of adverse effects the entire Chinese administrative system and China's currency will suffer. In the past ten weeks, the British and American ambassadors to Japan have repeatedly asked the Japanese government to curb smuggling in North China, but the Japanese government has paid little or no attention to it. The Japanese are now basing their actions on suspicion, economic oppression, and the general feelings of isolation from the world. The Japanese seem to be fighting the British because the British interests interfere with their own. However, recently many Japanese have felt the need to reach a general understanding with Britain.

Lord Peel then asked whether the British government could not carefully test the value of this feeling and sincerely ask Japan to explain its needs and negotiate an agreement that not only suits Japan but also includes the rights and happiness of China. He believes that this move can dispel all the clouds of suspicion in the Far East.

Lord Peel then mentioned the Soviet Russia's control of Outer Mongolia, asking whether Russia truly has an aggressive attitude. He believes that Japan's fear of Russia is partly hereditary and partly due to reality. One thing is clear now: the Japanese military's aggression against China is equivalent to driving China into Russia's arms. Lord Peel then described the extraordinary progress made by the Nanjing government in the past four years, saying that Japan can secure its market in China through friendly agreements. He was followed by former Under-Secretary of State for Foreign Affairs Lord Newton, who spoke in support of Japan, saying that Japan had been treated badly in Europe in the past forty years. The cancellation of the Anglo-Japanese Alliance and the misinformed intervention in Manchuria affairs, attempting to expel the Japanese from Manchuria, are particularly regrettable.

Next, Minister of Public Works Lord Stanhope rose to speak, saying that Japan has now increased its garrison in North China, making it extremely difficult for China to take action there. The situation in North China is very unstable, leading to a surge in smuggling. This is not only unfortunate for China but also harms all countries that trade with China. The British government has no intention of abandoning the British Embassy in Peiping but will maintain it. Another office of the embassy will be established in Nanjing. The British government is now focused on strengthening friendly relations with Japan. However, the current level has not yet reached the point where an agreement can be established because it is currently difficult to conclude a treaty that truly suits British policy in China. British policy in China is to maintain the Open Door Policy so that everyone has freedom of trade. The British desire to strengthen friendly relations with Japan has not been achieved due to recent incidents. "Manchukuo" has closed its doors and prohibited British trade. Other incidents, such as the mistreatment of Indian merchant couples in Changchun and the accusation of two British soldiers in Peiping, are all obstacles to the friendship between the two countries and prevent it from progressing. As for concluding a treaty, it is even more difficult. Now, in order to promote friendly relations with Japan and conclude a treaty that satisfies all three parties—China, Britain, and Japan—these incidents must be investigated to determine their cause. What Britain emphasizes is that China should have a strong and stable government. If it can be obtained, with the support of Japan and the United States, it will not only benefit China and Britain but also benefit Japan the most. Japan's trade with China accounts for a very large share. Lord Marley recently advocated that the League of Nations convene a conference to resolve the Sino-Japanese issue. He believes that the time is not yet ripe today. (20th Reuters Telegram)

(London) The House of Lords held a meeting today to discuss the Far East issue and the relations between Britain and Japan. Conservative Party member Lord Peel was the first to speak, saying that Britain has important interests in the Far East, so Britain must pay close attention to the changes in the situation there. He also said that when Sir Leith-Ross recently visited Japan, he heard the Japanese government provide assurances that Japan does not intend to interfere with China's international status. Conservative Party member Lord Newton spoke after Marley, defending Japan.

Minister of Public Works Lord Stanhope responded on behalf of the government, saying, "The situation in North China is very insecure, and as a result, smuggling has increased even more. This is unfortunate for both China itself and the countries engaged in trade with China. As for Japanese-Russian relations, the two sides have recently tried to demarcate the boundary between 'Manchukuo' and Outer Mongolia, and between 'Manchukuo' and the Soviet Union. If this work can be successful, the border disputes that have occurred repeatedly recently and are enough to cause danger can be expected not to be seen again. This also means that if we want to enhance the friendship between Britain and the countries in the Far East, we cannot allow these disputes to continue to occur. We should now try to establish a solution that not only satisfies us and Japan but also satisfies China," and so on. (20th Havas Telegram)

Germany's Military Expenditure Last Year Was 800 Million Pounds 37

(London) Chancellor of the Exchequer Chamberlain admitted in the House of Commons today that Churchill's estimate of Germany's military expenditure last year, reaching 800 million pounds, was not an exaggeration. (20th National Telegram)

British House of Commons Discusses Defense Budget; Seven-Eighths of Military Supplies Can Be Supplied by the Country 38

(London) The House of Commons met this afternoon to discuss the government's request for additional funding for the defense budget (totaling about 19 million pounds). First, Minister for Coordination of Defence Sir Thomas Inskip gave a long statement on the defense coordination work currently being carried out by the government, saying, with regard to the navy, the House of Commons can feel satisfied, and no party needs to be worried. With regard to the army, the reform started later than the air force, but since Sir Brown, the Director-General of Munitions Manufacture, took office, it can be accelerated. He also said that the sources of munitions have been discovered one after another, and the government has submitted contracts to 52 new factories to manufacture various munitions. Among them, 14 have accepted the contracts, and the production capacity of the remaining factories is being studied. He believes that seven-eighths of what the British army needs can be supplied by domestic factories. The government will set up a new arsenal in Nottingham, and the large arsenal in Woolwich will set up branches in Wales and Scotland. All these new factories will be under the jurisdiction of the Ministry for Coordination of Defence. With regard to the air force, some of the aircraft currently being manufactured are very fast. If they had been used in the Schneider Trophy race five years ago, it would not have been difficult to win the championship. After Inskip finished his speech, Labour Party member Smith spoke to criticize him, saying that the existing organization of the army, navy, and air force still lacks coordination and only increases waste. Conservative Party member Churchill also used his sharp words to criticize him severely, but his criticism was not directed at Inskip himself but at the powers exercised by Inskip, saying that once a war breaks out, the British economic system will collapse. The composition of this power is extremely absurd. The original initiators had no fixed opinions and no foresight. What they have achieved, although called the Ministry for Coordination of Defence, is actually a kind of committee, its internal complexity is like a maze. Even if Sir Thomas Inskip has talent, how can he display it? He (Churchill himself) believes that the government should urgently set up a Ministry of Munitions, but fears that this will not be realized until it is too late. (20th Havas Telegram)

International Intellectual Cooperation; Our Representative Speaks to the Committee 40

(Geneva) At the plenary meeting of the League of Nations International Committee on Intellectual Cooperation today, when discussing the issue of cooperation with China, the Chinese representative, Zhang Pengchun, stated that in order for any form of cooperation with China to be effective, it is imperative to understand China's intellectual habits and its recent trends. The two most important points are: (1) the form of China's cultural changes; (2) the new emotions of the Chinese student class. Regarding the first point, although opinions differ on China's cultural changes, all are deeply convinced of the complexity of the process. The lives of people of all classes in China are rapidly progressing in complexity, which cannot be stopped by narrow conservatism. The so-called "modernization" and "Westernization" are even less able to generalize this change. The forms that can be said to be obtainable are: (1) the concrete needs of reality can now be closely analyzed; (2) the historical facts of China, the West, ancient and modern, can seek what they jointly reveal; (3) creative aspects are rich in invention. All these forms are becoming increasingly apparent. In the past, international reports stated that the reforms in Chinese education seemed to be influenced by only one country. Fortunately, this situation has now become a thing of the past. As for the emotions of the Chinese student class, the most important points are: (1) the tense international situation has made students pay great attention to the country's military preparations. Chinese students are vigilant about the current crisis of the country, and their thinking is becoming more concrete, and they are prepared to receive strict training and take unified action at any time. (2) Chinese students are very interested in the farmers who account for 80% of China's population. Many educational institutions are directly active in various rural areas in the interior, and students all wish to go deep into the countryside and struggle from the bottom to create a new China. This is the most important trend, and there is no doubt about its profound impact. Zhang's speech was greatly praised by all parties, and the US representative was particularly impressed. After the meeting, he sent a letter expressing his admiration, saying that China's self-reliance and struggle have made the so-called silent transformation and beautification a thing of the past. Zhang is scheduled to give five lectures at the Geneva International Graduate Institute, then go to England, and then from England to the United States to participate in the annual meeting of the Pacific Cultural Association held in California. (20th Central News Agency Telegram)

Executive Yuan Decisions: Appointment of Song Ziliang Concurrently as Director of the Guangdong Department of Finance; Two Aviation Associations Decide to Merge with Five Agreed-Upon Measures; Approved National Assembly Expenses of 1.64 Million Yuan 49

(Nanjing) The Executive Yuan held its 272nd regular meeting on the morning of the 21st. Attendees included Kong Xiangxi, Jiang Zuobin, Huang Musong, Wu Dingchang, Chen Shaokuan, Zhang Jia'ao, Chen Shuren, He Yingqin, Wang Shijie, and Zhang Qun, with Kong Xiangxi presiding.

Reported Matters: (1) Secretary-General of the Yuan, Weng Wenhao, reported on two points discussed with the Examination Yuan: First, all agencies should strictly adhere to Article 5 of the Civil Servant Employment Law when employing personnel. If the proposed appointee's knowledge, experience, or health is not commensurate with the position, they should not be employed. The sequential filling of vacancies according to Article 17 of the Implementing Regulations of the Civil Servant Employment Law should also be handled according to the above principles. Second, the Examination Yuan will hold a special higher examination this year and intends to complete the examination before the opening of the employment guidance class for graduates of vocational schools and above on the 1st of the month. This is respectfully submitted for review. (2) Minister of Foreign Affairs presented a case that the League of Nations General Assembly has decided to lift sanctions against Italy on July 10th and requested that the Ministry of Finance be instructed to telegraph relevant agencies to cancel all sanctions against Italy from 00:00 on July 10th. A draft loan agreement was submitted for review and record. Resolution: First, the expenses for the National Assembly are set at 1,646,140 yuan. Second, the expenses for local elections will be drawn from the local governments' own reserve funds according to the standards proposed by the Ministry of Interior, or frugally from the budget for the current year. Provisional Organizational Outline for the Mongolian Political Affairs Committee in Chahar 51

(Nanjing) The Executive Yuan's meeting on the morning of the 21st approved the provisional organizational outline for the Mongolian League and Banner Group Local Autonomy Political Affairs Committee within Chahar Province, as well as a list of the chairman, vice-chairman, and committee members. The main points of the outline and the list are recorded below: (1) The League and Banner Group Local Autonomy Political Affairs Committee handles local autonomy affairs for the various banners under the Xilingol League, the four left-wing banners of Chahar, and the four pastoral groups. (2) The committee is directly subordinate to the Executive Yuan and is guided by the central competent authority. In case of matters involving the province, it shall consult with the provincial government. (3) The committee's location is in Jiabusi. (4) The committee consists of nine to twenty-four members, selected by the Executive Yuan from among the league leaders, deputy league leaders, Zhasakes, chief administrators, and other qualified personnel within Chahar Province, and appointed by the National Government. One member is designated as chairman and two as vice-chairman. (5) The committee meets once a month, and extraordinary meetings may be held when necessary. (6) The chairman of the committee implements the resolutions of the meetings in the preceding article, handles committee affairs, and supervises subordinate staff. The vice-chairmen take turns residing at the committee for six months each year, assisting the chairman in handling committee affairs. If the chairman is unable to perform his duties due to circumstances, the resident vice-chairman acts on his behalf. (7) The committee establishes seven departments: Secretariat, Counselor's Office, Civil Affairs, Industry, Education, Security, and Health, each in charge of various affairs. (8) Each department of the committee has one director, four secretaries, four counselors, twelve to sixteen section chiefs, and forty to sixty section members. (9) Eighteen councilors are appointed by the chairman from among the assistant administrators of each league and banner group. Permanent representatives residing at the committee liaise with and handle all affairs for their respective leagues and banner groups. When necessary, technical personnel and clerks may be employed.

List of Committee Members: Chairman Demchugdongrub, Vice-Chairmen Zhuotebazhapu, Linqinwangduet, Committee Members Songjinkewangchaoeke, Songnuodongluxi, Duoerji, Sangdakeduoerji, Butebole, Suotenamunuoerbu, Balagongsulong, Mukehuobao, Mengkedeqinggeer, Gongchukulashi, Yindehe, Temurboluote, Selengnamujile, Guoerzhuoerzhabu, Tuoketuhu. (Central News Agency, 21st)

Tianjin New Station: Customs Officers Seize Smuggled Goods; Strict Enforcement Unprecedented in Half a Year; Over Thirty Japanese Rōnin Scatter Upon Seeing the Opportunity 53

(Tianjin) At 11:00 PM on the 21st, Japanese rōnin transported 272 cases of artificial silk, 20 bags of sugar, and 4 pieces of broadcloth, all loaded onto the 3rd-class passenger carriage of the Tianjin-Pukou southbound train No. 305, occupying four sections. When the train arrived at the New Station from the East Station, Si Pusi, a customs officer from the Tianjin Customs Anti-Smuggling Station, A Qi, an anti-smuggling officer stationed in Tianjin from the Auxiliary Investigation Division, and over thirty Chinese and foreign customs officers directed dozens of porters and railway staff to unload the goods. Upon seeing the unfavorable situation, over thirty Korean rōnin accompanying the train scattered. The Japanese military police at the New Station did not make any statement. The customs officers hired five heavy-duty trucks to transport the goods to the customs warehouse for confiscation. This action was unprecedented in the past half year. The situation at the station was tense during the enforcement. Wang Xiting, the head of the Tianjin-Pukou Railway Police Department, led his troops to guard the station, and fortunately, there were no accidents. (Special dispatch, 21st)

(Tianjin) The Hebei-Chahar Committee believes that the Tianjin Customs Maritime Patrol Boat "Yu Guang" is being monitored, and maritime anti-smuggling efforts have been relaxed. It plans to restore the Cangzhou Maritime Defense Inspection Office to assist in anti-smuggling. An agreement is close, and effective measures may be promulgated soon. (Special dispatch, 21st)

Heavy Rains in Various Parts of Hebei; Five Major Rivers Rise Simultaneously; Dikes Are in Danger, and River Workers Are Rushing to Protect Them 56

(Tianjin) A heavy rain poured down in Tianjin from 00:00 this morning and stopped at 5:00 AM. The rainfall was the first of its kind since the beginning of summer. Two people surnamed Yu in the western suburbs were electrocuted and killed by lightning strikes. According to reports this morning, heavy rains fell in various counties of Hebei, and the five major rivers rose simultaneously. The dikes of the Yellow River and Taihang River are in danger. The Zhonghong Baping Canal of the Yongding River, and the Daqing and Hutuo Rivers overflowed their banks. Crops were flooded in Baoding. Several breaches occurred in the Ji Canal and Chaobai River. Downstream of the river, small boats were suspended. The South Canal's water level rose especially sharply, and residents were extremely panicked. Fortunately, the weather has cleared up, and it is hoped that there will be no danger. However, it is still muggy, and there is concern about more heavy rain. (Shenshi News Agency, 21st)

(Tianjin) At 5:00 PM on the 21st, the water level at the Lugouqiao Bridge on the Yongding River suddenly rose by two Chinese feet, reaching a height of fifteen feet. The water flow through the bridge openings was extremely swift. The south dike was also in danger. River workers were on the dikes guarding them. Due to the rain, the water level of the rivers around Tianjin rose sharply on the 21st. The City Flood Control Association ordered six anti-risk teams to rush to plug the rat holes and reinforce the dikes and embankments of the Beitu, Ziya, and other rivers, and requested the city government to allocate 50,000 yuan in anti-risk funds for emergency use. (Special dispatch, 21st)

(Tianjin) The water level of the South Canal continued to rise on the 21st, but the flow was still stable. The River Bureau received reports that the overflowing sections in Jiangmitun, Xiaoxinzhuang, Sanguanfu, and Shuipenzi in Wuqiao County, Jingxian County, and Dongguang County in the first section were plugged by gathering people to rush to block them. The breached section in Jiedicheng River in the third section is being rushed to block. On the 21st, the water level at Lian Town was 17.50 meters, an increase of 1.8 cm. The water level at Botou in the first section was 15.88 meters, an increase of 2.8 cm. Supervision committee member Liu Zhicheng and River Bureau Chief Li Binhu went to inspect and supervise the blocking of dangerous works on the 21st. (Special dispatch, 21st)

Tianjin British Concession: Rickshaw Pullers' Tax Resistance 58

(Tianjin) The Tianjin Rickshaw Association opposes the British Municipal Council's rickshaw inspection and tax collection methods. Starting on the morning of the 21st, the association issued a notice to all rickshaw factories to remove the British Concession tax licenses and refuse to operate in the concession. From morning to night, there was not a single rickshaw in the entire concession, causing great inconvenience to transportation. The connection between Special District One and the French Concession in Hebei Hedong was completely severed. Those who went to the British Concession for business had to walk. The British Municipal Council temporarily added vehicles and routes to the public bus line to maintain services. The Rickshaw Association submitted a petition to the municipal government on the 21st, stating that the rickshaw tax affects business, and they had no choice but to unanimously decide to resist the tax, urging the British Municipal Council to reflect and hope to withdraw the order. They will resume operations in the evening. The municipal government sent personnel to visit the British authorities, hoping they would not insist on their opinion. There are about 2,000 rickshaws in the British Concession. In the past, rickshaw owners paid the tax and obtained a tax license at any time, nailed it to the rickshaw, and could operate. The British authorities now feel this is cumbersome and have specified that starting from August 1st, each rickshaw factory will have to pull the rickshaws to the bureau once a day to inspect the vehicles and issue licenses, to avoid abuses and eliminate trouble. The Rickshaw Association has appealed for many days without effect, and finally decided to use the negative strategy of resisting the tax. It is said that there are 5,000 rickshaw drivers in the industry. Officials are paying close attention to this. The attitude of the British authorities is still firm and there is no sign of change. (Special dispatch, 21st)

Chengde Under Japanese Rule: Years of Cultivating a Cultural Capital, Now Controlled by the Japanese at Will 62

Chengde Correspondence: Chengde means "Rehe" in Mongolian, which is the administrative center of Rehe Province. The city is located among mountains. To the east are the Panying, Luohan, Tianqiao, and Five Fingers Mountains; to the west are the Fengyun and Guangren Mountains; to the south are the Sengguan, Qingsong, and Fenghuang Mountains; and to the north are the Lion Ridge and Daheishan Mountains. The city is surrounded by mountains. The Rehe River flows from the southeast end of the city to the southwest end, meeting at the Dahe River three miles southwest of Rehe. The cultural capital that has been cultivated for many years is the unique composition of Chengde. Since the Japanese occupation, the Japanese have actively developed industries. According to Japanese surveys, the population and number of households are as follows:

Number of Households Population

(Relationship with Japan) After the Northeast Incident, the Japanese army actively sought to invade the Rehe region. After the conflict broke out, many Japanese soldiers died. The Japanese now consider this to be a place with a deep impression on the Japanese army. The Japanese Kwantung Army considers Chengde to be the most important place. Since last year, a large loyal spirit tower has been built using the latest architectural style, scheduled to be completed in Showa 12 (1937). The main institutions of the Japanese side, such as the consulate and group headquarters, are concentrated here. The main ones are: (1) Consulate, (2) Same Police Department, (3) Group Headquarters, (4) Military Police Headquarters, (5) Special Affairs Agency, (6) Mantetsu (South Manchuria Railway) Office, (7) Resident Association, (8) Elementary School, (9) Telecommunications Company, (10) Joseon Bank Branch Office, (11) Aviation Company Branch Office, (12) International Transportation Company Branch Office, (13) Rehe New Newspaper Office. Transportation in and near the city includes rickshaws, camel litters, railway bureau automobiles, and airplanes. The General Bureau operates automobiles connecting Fengning, Weichang, Gubeikou. Airplanes connect Lingyuan, Chaoyang, Jin County, etc., which is even more important than Mudanjiang in eastern Manchuria.

(Industrial Value) The composition of the Chengde industrial market has a very close relationship with the establishment of the Rehe provincial government. In the past, the products of Rehe were concentrated in Chengde. To give an example: (1) Phoebe wood is transported through Gubeikou, Pingquan, Chaoyang, and Beipiao, using the transportation of the Yan River, and exported to Pingjin and Fengtian, with an annual output of 1.47 million yuan. (2) White pears are moved in from Maogou Gongfu in Longhua and exported to Weichang, Chifeng, and Linxi. (3) Charcoal is imported from Shangbancaizhuang and Zhuangtouyingzi. (4) Leather is imported and exported to China through Gubeikou. Although it is produced near Chengde, it is mostly a collection and distribution center for leather from various places. (5) Carpets and rugs are transported through Pingquan, Chaoyang, and Gubeikou as transportation hubs. (6) Coal is produced within the county and is only used to meet the needs of the county. The importance of the industrial market is not difficult to infer.

Lu Province's Third Phase of Abolishing Exorbitant and Miscellaneous Taxes, and Reducing Additional Land Taxes in Wudi and Eight Other Counties 63

Jinan Dispatch: The Shandong Province government, following orders to abolish exorbitant taxes and miscellaneous levies, has already abolished two phases, totaling over 329,000 yuan. Now, starting from July 1st, the third phase, amounting to nearly 200,000 yuan, is being abolished. The additional land taxes in Wudi and eight other counties, which were excessively heavy, are also being reduced. For every yuan of regular tax, the shortfall will be compensated by 40% of the stamp tax revenue allocated to the province by the central government. The remaining amount to be abolished is over 790,000 yuan, which will be abolished when compensatory funds become available in the future. In addition to issuing public notices to inform the public about the abolition of the third phase of exorbitant and miscellaneous taxes, the provincial government has also submitted a report to the Ministry of Finance for record-keeping. The Ministry of Finance has replied, approving the record-keeping and expressing commendation. The following is a list of the counties where the additional land tax exceeds the regular tax by the largest amount, showing the amount to be reduced progressively: Wudi, with a tax rate of 1.713 li per yuan, should levy 89.076 yuan, should reduce 1.400 yuan. Feixian, with a tax rate of 1.849 li per yuan, should levy 91.229 yuan, should reduce 17.219 yuan, and after reduction, should levy 74.010 yuan. Mengyin, with a tax rate of 1.558 li per yuan, should levy 56.885 yuan, should reduce 2.118 yuan, and after reduction, should levy 54.767 yuan. Fanxian, with a tax rate of 1.620 li per yuan, should levy 69.336 yuan, should reduce 5.136 yuan, and after reduction, should levy 64.200 yuan. Puxian, with a tax rate of 2.428 li per yuan, should levy 59.768 yuan, should reduce 22.844 yuan, and after reduction, should levy 36.924 yuan. Rongcheng, with a tax rate of 1.798 li per yuan, should levy 67.466 yuan, should reduce 11.182 yuan, and after reduction, should levy 56.284 yuan. Dingtao, with a tax rate of 1.529 li per yuan, should levy 103.129 yuan, should reduce 1.956 yuan, and after reduction, should levy 101.173 yuan. The total amount to be levied is 598.289 yuan, the amount to be reduced is 72.931 yuan, and after the reduction, the amount to be levied is 525.358 yuan. The additional land taxes levied in the first and second phases in the above eight counties, as included in the local budget案 for the 24th year of the Republic, exceeded 1 yuan and 5 jiao per yuan of regular tax. That is, the additional tax levied per tael of Dingyin (poll tax silver) exceeded 6 yuan. The burden on the people was indeed too heavy. It is now proposed to follow the regulations promulgated by the Ministry and adopt a progressive reduction policy, temporarily reducing it to 1 yuan and 5 jiao additional tax per yuan of regular tax, i.e., 6 yuan additional tax per tael of Dingyin. If compensatory funds become available in the future, further reductions will be considered.

Songjiang: Investigating a Male Corpse with Knife Wounds 64

On the 18th of this month, an unidentified male corpse with knife wounds was discovered behind the Gu Family's Righteous Burial Ground in Huayang Bridge. The cause of death has been the subject of much speculation and uncertainty. Investigation revealed that the deceased, Sun Xinquan, was married to a woman named Huang. Last year, Huang had an affair with Yao Youcai, and Sun exercised his marital rights by reporting the affair to the court. The court found Yao Youcai and Huang guilty of adultery and sentenced them to imprisonment. They have now been released after serving their sentences. The sudden murder of Sun Xinquan is highly suspicious. After the incident, his wife, Huang, and her lover, Yao Youcai, fled together, further increasing suspicion. The prosecutor's office has dispatched judicial police chief Xue Bingzhang to the location of the coffin to open it in the presence of the Fourth Police Station to photograph the deceased for investigation.

Taicang: Robbery and Assault at an Open-Air Temple 66

Recently, bandits have been rampant in the four rural areas of this county, looting and injuring people. It has been heard from time to time. At around 2 AM yesterday morning, more than ten bandits suddenly arrived at the home of Pui Sunquan, the chief of the village in the open-air temple area of the county's second district. Speaking in mixed accents and wielding weapons, they broke down the front door and forced the family members into one room, tying them up one by one and warning them not to make any noise. Jiading: The Chamber of Commerce Telegraphs Against Income Tax 67

To the National Federation of Chambers of Commerce, the Federation of Chambers of Commerce of each province, and the Chambers of Commerce of each city, county, district, and town: It is reported that the Legislative Yuan has passed the Provisional Income Tax Regulations, which will be implemented soon. Income tax is considered a good tax system in Western countries, using the surplus of the people to supplement the needs of the state. There is no need to be stubborn when the people and the state are mutually supportive. If the people are rich, how can the state not be rich? There is no need to question this any further. However, among the scholars, farmers, workers, and merchants in our country, those who can be considered wealthy because of the country's advocacy, maintenance, and protection are few. Considering the balance, we are still in a transitional period where scholars cannot find employment, workers have no jobs, businesses are sluggish, and the countryside is bankrupt. However, if the state cannot delay the collection of this income tax, then compassion must be incorporated into the collection process. The purpose of Premier Sun's ambition to relieve the people's suffering must be considered in this tax collection. The main points are as follows: Regarding the first category, income from profit-making businesses, considering the small shops in the interior, assuming that they only have 5% to less than 10% of their actual capital as annual income, but considering the expenses of their family life, the business surplus is not enough to offset it. (According to the interior shop, this type is actually more common) Then, comprehensively speaking, the result is still that income does not offset expenses. Even if the tax is small, it still increases the people's debt. Regarding the second category, income from salaries and remuneration, the average starting point for taxation is 30 to 60 yuan per month. This is only considering the individual's perspective, but who does not have a family? Assuming a family of five or seven, with women, children, and the elderly all relying on one person for livelihood, occasional illnesses and deaths, social interactions, and temporary mandatory donations from the state and local governments, those who have even a little public spirit and decency must borrow to make ends meet. Their suffering is unspeakable. Collecting income tax is truly beyond their means. Regarding the third category, income from savings deposits, having savings deposits seems to indicate affluence. However, the actual situation in the country is that many orphans, widows, and impoverished people cannot support themselves and rely on a small amount of inherited savings or the support of relatives and friends to pool funds, forming savings societies to earn interest to subsidize their livelihoods. (If these savings deposits encounter bankruptcy, they are likely to die) Taxing this is equivalent to taking away their food. In short, it is easy to legislate, but there are many obstacles. The state's income from taxation should not deviate from the principle of using surplus to help the needy. May we ask for your agreement on the following: the first category, income from profit-making, should be taxed only on those that exceed 20% of its actual capital. As for the second category, those with a monthly income of less than 100 yuan should be taxed. The third category, interest on savings deposits, should be taxed only on those with an annual income exceeding 500 yuan. The percentage ratio of the tax rates for these three categories should be earnestly requested to be reduced as much as possible, so that the state's good tax can be collected, and the people will happily contribute. Today, the people are all aware of their obligations, but their ability to bear the burden is too weak. This is but a humble opinion. If it is deemed appropriate, please consider and adopt it, co-sign it to be presented to the superiors, so that the people's desires can be heard. Wang Wangnong, Chairman of the Jiading County Chamber of Commerce in Jiangsu, Jin Boqin, Pan Jisong, Wu Bingshen, and Song Hexing, Standing Committee Members, respectfully request.

Wuxi: The Silk Workers' Strike Completely Resolved 68

The silk factory strike in this county has been resolved after repeated persuasion by the Party and government authorities. Regarding the issues of improving treatment and increasing wages, Magistrate Long and Provincial Special Commissioner Zhang Gong, among others, invited representatives from both labor and management to a meeting yesterday to discuss the matter. The following was decided: (1) Working hours: start work at 5:15 AM and finish work at 6:00 PM (15 minutes for breakfast, 1 hour for lunch). (2) Wage standards: standard wage of 4 jiao 7 fen per day, minimum wage of 3 jiao 5 fen. (3) Year-end bonus of two and a half months' wages. (4) Standards for suspending work in hot weather: if the temperature inside the factory is above 96 degrees, stop work in the afternoon for half a day. (5) The salaries of factory staff and furnace workers will be increased at the discretion of each factory. Both labor and management expressed acceptance and dispersed. As for the arrested workers, if it is confirmed that they were not inciting the strike, the county will submit a request to the Second District Security Command to release them after questioning. The labor-management dispute, which had been delayed and unresolved, has now been completely resolved.

Wheat Boat Robbed En Route 69

He Xida, a resident of Luoyang Town in the sixth district of Wujin County, loaded over sixty stones of wheat onto a boat the day before yesterday, intending to sell it to Yong Shengyuan Rice Shop in Sanliqiao, Laiyi. Afterwards, He Xida sailed the boat to the city and reported the loss to the Public Security Bureau, requesting a thorough investigation.

Drug Trafficking Ring Cracked 74

According to a confidential report, the Nantong County Public Security Bureau discovered a drug trafficking ring on Tiaogang Road. Director Song sent secret agents to purchase drugs at the address, obtained morphine, and arrested the drug trafficker Sun Xingbang, who was a detective in the water police team. He was handed over to the District Security Command for interrogation.

Jiaxing: More Smuggled Goods Seized 75

On the 18th, the Jiahe Cloth Factory on West River Street, Jiaxing, seized twenty-one boxes of smuggled bleaching powder and over a thousand packages of Japanese yarn. While the case was still being handled by the county, on the 20th, Chen Hua, a policeman from the special service team of the Public Security Bureau, saw the Xie Shun Dyeing Workshop on Chunbo Bridge, West River Street, carrying thirty-one tins of paint and two bags of bleaching powder transported by the Tiansheng Transport Company from Tangwan Street and sold by the Yuanyuhe Paint Company in Shanghai. They only had invoices but no transit permit or distribution license. Considering them smuggled goods, he reported to the officer Wang Qiqing, who went to investigate and detained the goods and the dye shop owner, Kong A'ming, and sent them to the Public Security Bureau. Subsequently, someone bailed out Kong. The case will be reported to the county government for handling. As for the Jiahe Cloth Factory incident, Gu Suming, the chairman of the County Chamber of Commerce, has appealed strongly to Xian Yixian, the county magistrate. At the same time, Zhou Yuqing, the manager, is trying to prove in Shanghai that the goods were brought to He after inspection, which should not be difficult to resolve.

Hangzhou: Rioting Fishermen Escorted to the Province 76

The case of the riot by fishermen in Dinghai has been suppressed after the provincial government sent a large team of tax police and the Second Brigade of the Security Police's Water Police to suppress it. A large number of rioting fishermen sailed back to their native Fenghua on over a hundred fishing boats. When they arrived at Dapu Estuary, they were discovered by the tax police. The two sides exchanged fire. The tax police fired with machine guns, and the fishermen, unable to resist, scattered and fled. Five fishing boats and over twenty fishermen were captured and escorted to the province on the 21st, where they will be interrogated by the Liangzhe Transportation Commissioner to investigate the main culprits and punish them severely. The Daishan field office urgently needs to be restored. Deputy Director Yu Bingxun of the tax police has been specially appointed to act as the field director. Yu set off for Daishan on the morning of the 21st to resume the process of weighing and collecting taxes in order to maintain the livelihood of the fisherman.

The Water Level of the Qiantang River Recedes Slightly: Due to continuous heavy rain, the water level of the Qiantang River has risen sharply, about two meters higher than before in recent days. The dikes are in a dangerous state. The Construction Department should specially instruct the engineering team to strengthen protection to avoid accidents. Fortunately, the weather cleared on the 21st, and the water level dropped to 7.35 meters, easing the situation. The Qiantang River Bridge project is still proceeding as usual.

Ningbo: The Daishan Riot Case Subsides 77

The riot of supervisors and fishermen in Daishan, Dinghai, has subsided. Zhang Zhongli, the director of the tax police bureau, arrived in Ningbo from Hangzhou yesterday. Today, he will go to Daishan with Commissioner Zhao to investigate the truth of the incident. Regarding this riot, he advocates punishing the instigators. Wu Yizeng, the fifth district assistant stationed in the tax office, came to Ningbo yesterday to report that five tax policemen had died and three were injured. Team leader Hu Bugui was killed, and four people, including Cheng Taikang and Yang Shangdong, were also killed. The rest have not yet been identified. The position of director of the Daishan field office and director of the weighing and releasing bureau will be held concurrently by Yu Bingxun, the deputy director of the tax police bureau. To increase its strength and suppress the rioters, the tax police bureau has borrowed the Jian'an warship from Qingdao and the Huaibei warship from Haizhou to patrol Dinghai, and telegraphed the independent battalion of the tax police headquarters stationed in Haimen, Linhai, to send a company of soldiers to suppress the area. It has also received 1,000 of the latest Han-made 79 rifles, 20 machine guns, and 200,000 rounds of ammunition from the Ministry of Finance, which will be distributed to the tax police teams in various places to increase their strength (20th).

Shaoxing: Various Legal Groups Discuss Deed Tax 78

Regarding the case of deed tax inspection in Shaoxing, various legal groups, including the Yue Social County Chamber of Commerce, have submitted reports requesting relief, stating the actual difficulties and proposed solutions. On the 20th, the county government convened representatives from various legal groups to discuss solutions and decided: (1) Temporarily suspend door-to-door deed inspections. (2) The county government will re-request the provincial finance department to extend the period for voluntary tax payment without penalty until the end of August. (3) For property owners with only white deeds (unregistered deeds), if the deeds are not in Shaoxing or if they cannot raise funds in time, they may first report the location of the property, the date of the deed, the number of deeds, the deed price, the price of the already taxed deeds, the number of untaxed white deeds, the deed price, and the scheduled date of tax payment to the deed tax office. Within the deadline (the deadline cannot exceed two weeks), even if a complaint is filed, it will not be accepted. However, if the tax is not paid after the deadline, they will still be summoned and penalized.

Taizhou: Rice Worms Spread for Thirty Li 79

The inchworm has recently been discovered to be severe in the eastern rural areas of Wenyu, including Lang'ao, Niuqiao, Houzeng, Mache Bridge, Gaoyuan, Xinhe, Tangxia, and Siqian Bridge. The early and late rice crops in the fields are almost completely eaten. The early rice harvest is feared to be less than half of what it should be. The late rice stalks and leaves are all gone, leaving only the rice roots. The people's food prospects are greatly affected. To understand the situation, the reporter went to various places to investigate and learned that the area of affected fields has spread for as much as thirty li. Farmers are all worried and sighing.

Anecdotes of the Southern Inspection Tour: Qu County, an Important Town in Eastern Zhejiang 80

— Special Correspondent Shi Ying of this Newspaper

Qu County is an important place in the mountainous area of eastern Zhejiang, bordering Fujian, Jiangxi, and Anhui. Its position in eastern Zhejiang is somewhat like an outlying corner with Jinhua and Lishui. Jinhua and Lishui are also important places in eastern Zhejiang, but not as important as Qu County in terms of inter-provincial significance. In the future, when the Beijing-Quzhou Railway is built and meets the Zhejiang-Jiangxi Railway here, looking towards Nanjing and Shanghai, this place will be precisely at the apex of a narrow equilateral triangle, and its position will become increasingly important. This can be imagined intuitively.

The county was formerly known as the Quzhou Prefecture Seat, and because the major roads of Fujian, Jiangxi, and Anhui provinces converge in Qu County, it is also known as Sanqu. It governs five counties, including Jiangshan and Changshan. Now, a commissioner's office and security command are established, and its jurisdiction has increased by two counties compared to the past. At the beginning of the Qing Dynasty, the large army conquered Quzhou, followed by the Eight Min regions. Later, when the Revolt of the Three Feudatories broke out, Governor-General Li Zhifang rushed to guard this city, and Geng Jingzhong was ultimately unable to succeed. During the Taiping Rebellion, Zuo Zongtang mobilized troops from various provinces and also used this place as a base for attacking the Taiping rebels. During the Fujian Incident in the 22nd year of the Republic of China, although the situation slightly changed due to the overnight expansion of the Hangzhou-Jiangshan Road and its opening to traffic in Jiangshan, Qu County's strategic location meant it had earlier access to transportation. Adequate preparations were made in military supplies, which also boosted the morale of the soldiers at the front.

The city of Qu County was built under the supervision of Tang dynasty imperial guard Chi Jingde. It is surrounded by water on three sides and backed by mountains on one side. There are many paddy fields inside the city. During the Taiping Rebellion, it was besieged for three years, and the people cultivated the land to supply the army with food, and it was never lost. Therefore, it is known as "Iron Quzhou." However, the city is not very high. In this era of three-dimensional warfare, the golden cities and moats of the past are no longer sufficient to rely on. The headquarters of the 18th Army, stationed in the city, adapted to the needs of the times. In addition to military engineering, building roads, and opening new city gates, they also actively promoted public health. Recently, they also held a grand air defense exercise, using the appeal of a lantern festival to attract even people from the countryside to come and see what was going on. This is probably a very meaningful pioneering effort in the counties of the mountainous area of eastern Zhejiang.

Luo Zhuoying, the commander of the 18th Army, is brave, good at strategy, and respected by senior generals. He is praised as a rising star. Through the introduction of my old friend Yang Xingzhi, a lieutenant colonel secretary in the command, I had the opportunity to chat with Luo about issues such as external bandit suppression and the movements in Guangdong and Guangxi. He spoke eloquently for more than an hour, and I was very impressed. I will select what can be mentioned and briefly describe it. Luo believes that in terms of foreign affairs, once a punch is thrown, it must be done with certainty and strength. Years of bandit suppression have reduced the country's strength, which is a great regret. He used the army's deployment in eastern Zhejiang as an example, stating that its main purpose was not to suppress the remaining bandits. However, in the past year, the troops under his command have rarely been completely isolated from suppression work. Although this is a minor distraction, they are still diligently preparing for the current movements in Guangdong and Guangxi. If the Second Plenary Session of the Kuomintang's Central Executive Committee cannot resolve the matter through political means, the central government, for the sake of national unity, may have to suppress the rebellion. His words were filled with emotion. Later, I was invited to dinner by Zhuang Mingyuan, the director of the secretariat, with Zhu Yulin, the chief of staff, and others as companions. They provided a lot of information, and their kindness was appreciated. Later, I left Qu County and heard that the army was also transferred to southern Jiangxi. Looking up to the situation in Lingnan, the clouds are becoming increasingly dark. I would like to sincerely say to the generals on both sides that if this time they cannot turn hostility into friendship, and if brothers are forced to meet on the battlefield, they should fire as few bullets as possible and preserve as much strength as possible, because these two large expenditures are not like spending someone else's money. The results will all be recorded in the family's accounts, and they must be vigilant against the final days of bankruptcy.

The total population of Qu County is about 300,000, of which the Jiangshan and Jiangxi groups each account for almost one-third. Due to the water conservancy of the 72 ditches and the adjustment between highlands and lowlands, even in years of drought or flood, it is only a minor disaster. The ownership of the land originally belonged entirely to the local people, but because they were fond of eating and lazy, they hired foreigners as tenants. They worked diligently and frugally, and after many years, the ownership of the land in the hands of the landlords was mostly transferred to the tenants, and it implicitly became "farmers own their land." Currently, due to the excessive surcharges on taxes and the implementation of the "25% rent reduction," the price of land has fallen, and very few transactions are completed. However, the "25% rent reduction" has suppressed the collapse of a part of the poor farmers. Although it is not unfavorable to the landlords, it is still a good policy. The main products are rice and paper, followed by firewood, charcoal, Dahongqiao timber, etc.

There is a place called "Ten Mile Barren Mountain" where the Zhejiang Construction Department has reclaimed 10,000 mu of land and planted more than 1.3 million tung trees. The district office took over the management, and after three years, when the oil is produced, it can yield a profit of 600,000 to 700,000 yuan per year, which is a great source of wealth. It is said that the monthly management fee of 400 yuan is difficult to raise, and they want to transfer prisoners from various counties to do the farming work, but because they cannot find guarantors, it is difficult to realize, which is a pity. However, in this world, there can never be only benefits without disadvantages. Prisoner reclamation has great benefits and few disadvantages. Why be so particular about guarantees? Moreover, if the planting of tung trees is successful, giving them some benefits would move even the most stubborn prisoners. If there are inevitably shortcomings in the implementation, in order to complete the great plan of planting tung trees, letting a few lucky prisoners slip through the net should be regarded as a general amnesty, which is also worthwhile.

The banditry in the surrounding counties has not been completely suppressed. There are groups of three or five, and there are also groups of dozens of people, running around like wolves, wandering aimlessly. The large army's suppression has no obvious target, and because they do not communicate with the bandits, they are secretly afraid of them, or at least they dare not offend them. Even the baojia chiefs dare not take the position. It is as difficult to get them to report bandit activities to the government troops as it is to snatch walnuts from a monkey's mouth. The kidnapping of wealthy people and attacks on local militias by bandits are silent and invisible beforehand. With a single signal, it erupts, and often it is impossible to distinguish between bandits and civilians, and it is impossible to distinguish between the enemy and ourselves. In a hurry, they do not know what to do. On the morning of the 8th of this month, Kaihua County was once attacked and captured by more than 400 bandits, and there was no clue to be found beforehand. Therefore, at present, political work is more important than military affairs in the suppression work, that is, implementing the so-called "90% politics, 10% military affairs," actively engaging in organizing the baojia, training the militia, and promoting grain storage. In particular, the item of grain storage, when the price of newly harvested grain falls, farmers can pledge to the grain storage to borrow money and sell it when the grain price rises, which is of great benefit to adjusting the rural economy, and national defense food can also be fully prepared in advance, so the promotion is quite vigorous and the results are obvious. It can be seen that the purpose is only limited to suppressing the remaining bandits.

In the city of Qu County, there is a Southern Lineage Confucius Temple, where the portraits of Confucius and his wife Guan Shi are enshrined. It is said that they were hand-carved by Zigong from ebony wood. During the Southern Song Dynasty, they were brought to Quzhou by Kong Duanyou, the Duke Yansheng, and have been treasured to this day. I submitted a card to visit. The two statues are each more than a foot high, sitting side by side. Confucius faces forward, holding a jade tablet, with a dark complexion and vigorous carving. When tapped, it makes the sound of metal and stone. It is said to have become petrified ebony. The current sacrificial official is one generation older than Kong Decheng of the Northern Lineage. He once entered a Japanese military academy and indulged in prostitution and gambling, which was dissatisfying to the clan. The sacrificial official was originally supposed to receive a monthly salary of 400 yuan from the government, but to date, for two or three years, not even a copper coin has been received.

In the Juzhang Hotel where I stayed in Qu County, I saw several old and elegant paintings on the wall. The signature was Wang, the owner of the hotel. I had heard of finger painting, but I had never seen it. Fortunately, this old finger painter used to be in the same industry as me. More than ten years ago, he ran a small newspaper in Shanghai. He said that at that time, the Newspaper Association was attached to the Shen Bao, and he often went there. When I went to see him at this time, we seemed like old acquaintances as soon as we met. Knowing my intentions, the old man spread out a piece of rice paper, dipped ink with his middle finger, and quickly painted a picture of a pine tree and sent it to me. Moreover, when it was finished, it was read to add to the fun. It is said that in finger painting, it is important to use unusual and risky strokes and to use raw paper (without sizing) for painting, so that it will not change for a long time. Gao Qipei (号且圆), a Grand Secretary of the early Qing Dynasty, was able to do this, so he was imitated by finger painters, but very few can use raw paper, and the elegance of the ink is also different. I tried to paint a few strokes, but my finger was bald and could not be sharpened, and there was no way to pour ink into it. Those who are good at finger painting can freely control the shading and perspective, which can be said to be another unique skill in the art world.
