Shanghai Newspaper's National Products Special Edition

A Word of Contribution

Productivity and Consumption 141

— Yang An

The most important way to promote and popularize national products is to increase the purchasing power of the general public, and the driving force behind increasing purchasing power lies in the consumption power of the general public. How to ensure everyone has the power to consume means fostering everyone's productivity.

Those living below the poverty line do not have the power to consume, so how can they have purchasing power? After investigating the reasons, it is because of the bankruptcy of rural areas and the underdevelopment of industry and commerce, resulting in everyone lacking productivity.

Because there is no productivity, people can only make do with clothing, food, housing, and transportation, so where is the power to supply consumption? No matter how good or suitable the goods are, where is the power to buy them? Weak consumption power leads to decreased purchasing power, and the things produced have no way out. Cause and effect are mutually generated, as if containing a cycle. Therefore, to enable everyone to have consumption power and purchasing power, we must stimulate the productivity of the general public in the interior.

Recently, the National Economic Movement has focused on promoting national products, especially various sideline occupations in the interior. This is the best way to promote productivity. Farmers spend less than half of the year actually cultivating the land, and the remaining half can be used to develop sideline occupations, increasing everyone's productivity and naturally increasing purchasing power. This is the prerequisite for promoting national products and is worth paying attention to.

Hoping that Students Will Work Hard on National Products during the Summer Vacation 142

— Xuan Wan

After reading Mr. Yang Yao's article in the last issue of this journal, I feel very moved by the "Summer Vacation Student National Products Movement". Indeed, in these days of national crisis, especially with severe smuggling, which has put the national economy at risk and caused the entire industrial sector to move towards total collapse day by day, it is extremely urgent and important to propose to students across the country to use their vacation to work hard on the national products movement. At the same time, I believe that students across the country will certainly be unwilling to let the great time pass by in vain in this extraordinary period, but will take this opportunity to do some very meaningful and valuable things. Therefore, they will definitely not hesitate to work hard on and diligently promote this basic work of saving the country—the national products movement.

Recently, the Shanghai National Products Movement United Association hosted the education and news circles last week to discuss the implementation of summer student national products work and established a summer student national products promotion association, which passed its regulations and work outline. This is a piece of news that is worth everyone's joy. We hope that teachers and students in elementary, middle, and high schools across the country will immediately respond to it and expand it. In particular, every student returning to their hometown should pay attention to being able to adapt to the needs of each local environment and carry out their work accordingly. Below, I would also like to write down a few points that I consider most important in the work for reference:

1. In your hometown, work hard to publicize the benefits of using national products and the dangers of smuggling and the harm of dumping foreign goods, using the most alerting words or writing to persuade all the villagers. In the morning or evening, it is best to use the villagers' spare time to hold national products speeches at various public gathering places, such as teahouses, hotels, temples, etc.

2. Conduct a detailed survey of the promotion of national products and the encroachment of smuggling on the country's industrial and commercial sectors in your hometown.

3. Collect various exquisite national product exhibits and hold mobile national product exhibitions in your hometown.

4. Go to various retail stores in your hometown to persuade store owners to sell only national products and no longer import foreign goods to meet market needs.

5. Investigate the comparison of national and foreign product sales and the degree of smuggling prevalence in your hometown. Compile numerical statistics and publicize them to the public locally to raise awareness. At the same time, make detailed records for compilation in the report.

In short, we believe that all the respectable and lovable students across the country will be willing to work hard on this meaningful work of saving the country, and will make the future of the Citizen National Products Year shine with a different color.

Talking About Yixing Pottery 143

— Wan Naijun

It can be said that the Chinese people do not love and protect domestic products enough, regardless of their size! Now, let's point out and talk about Yixing pottery. Regarding its nature, function, aesthetics, and value, it all conforms to economic principles. These are described below:

There are many types of pottery products, including teapots, teacups, tea bowls, flower vases, flowerpots, antique bottles, tripods, stationery, toys, and so on. Even for each type of product, there are at least twenty to thirty color and size varieties, and as many as forty to fifty. Furthermore, product names such as teapots, flower vases, and tripods are meaningful and mostly historically evaluated. The soil is sticky, pure, and durable, and will never be as easily broken as foreign goods, which are not uniformly made inside and out.

In terms of function, they become antiques over time and are said to be difficult to break. For example, teapots, after many years, can keep water in the pot from ever developing a strange taste! Flowerpots, after a considerable number of years, make it easier to grow flowers and plants in the pot. There are too many to list.

The colors are purple, yellow, dark green, and red. The colors are glossy and bright, especially dark green, which is more valuable. Furthermore, specially made tea bowls and flower pots with broken porcelain surfaces are even more elegant. Regardless of color or size, they are far superior to the ceramics of Western goods.

The price of each product, although there are also expensive ones worth several tens of yuan, of course, these are precious ones; but there are also cheap and beautiful ones starting from one dime. They can be suitable for the strength of purchasing power.

Chinese people: Understand this. Buying foreign goods is not only losing the responsibility and obligation of a citizen. You should also know, why bother to spend your money to bring many guns to hit our motherland for foreign chimneys! No, let's say hitting yourself.

Here I advise my compatriots to happily use the quintessence of national pottery, happily use all domestic products, and not allow rights to leak out; it is also a virtue.

Sports News

The Olympic Torch Relay Begins: Solemn and Grand Ceremony Reaches Unprecedented Heights; Expected to Arrive in Bulgaria on Thursday 147

Athens, July 20th (Reuters) – The first ceremony of the Olympic Games, the lighting of the sacred flame in ancient Olympia, commenced today. After the flame was lit, the 3,000-mile torch relay race across six European countries also began. The final runner will arrive in Berlin on August 1st, the opening day of the Games, to light the Olympic fire.

At 8:00 AM this morning, the flame was lit using sunlight, and twelve maidens carried it to a special altar, chanting Pindar's Olympic oath. The first runner, a resident of Mount Olympia named Condylis, repeated the oath once more. After lighting his torch from the flame on the altar, he began the first stage of his journey. Each runner will run approximately one kilometer. More than 3,000 runners will participate, and the relay is expected to reach the Bulgarian border on Thursday.

King George of Greece also attended the solemn ceremony at the Olympic stadium, which was lavishly decorated to welcome the participating runners.

Unprecedented Grandeur

National Maritime News Agency, July 20th, Ancient Olympia – This morning, crowds thronged the road to the Temple of Ars to witness the torch relay. The torch relay, from Mount Olympus to the Berlin Olympic Games, began at 10:00 AM this morning. The first torch was lit using a concave mirror to focus sunlight. Long before the start, students from various schools, government officials, and other spectators had gathered at the designated locations to wait. The commemorative plaque presented by Baron de Coubertin in 1934 was also hung beside the Temple of Ars. A special altar was built next to the temple, where the first relay runner began his run.

Baron's Speech

This morning, Baron de Coubertin, the founder of the Olympic Games, delivered a speech at the start of the torch relay here. He briefly stated that fifty years ago, he planned a youth education system, but he firmly believed that political or social methods were inferior to physical education methods. Hence, this great movement was initiated. "Physical training not only makes a great contribution to public health but also greatly helps in personal outlook on life. The most notable effect is making young people smile often, thus conquering difficulties becomes effortless."

Bishop's Blessing

While celebrating the first torch relay race at Mount Olympus, Earl de Coubertin recited a speech and led the athletes in taking the Olympic oath. Following this, Bishop Apikagos stood up to give a blessing, saying, "May God's will, which is the light of the people, follow this torch to Germany. Furthermore, may the spirit of Christianity be transmitted to the friendly German people. At the same time, may the burning of this torch represent the enthusiasm of the world's national athletes in their pursuit of God's glory."

Berlin Celebrations

National Maritime News Agency, July 20th, Berlin – This afternoon, a grand gathering was held in the Berlin City Hall to celebrate the start of the torch relay in ancient Olympia.

Dr. Lewald, President of the Olympic Organizing Committee, presented a beautifully carved wooden torch to Berlin Mayor Lippert, expressing gratitude for the Mayor's contributions to the preparations for the Olympic Games. Subsequently, the Greek flag was raised in the main hall of the City Hall, and the Greek national anthem was played. Other athletic events were participated in.

Vocational Training Classes for Graduates from Colleges and Above: The Executive Yuan Approved the Results of the Preparatory Committee Meeting Yesterday; Recruiting 1,000 Students for Four Months of Training with Subsidies 165

(Central News Agency, Nanjing, July 21st) The results of the second meeting of the Preparatory Committee for the Vocational Training Classes for Graduates from Colleges and Above were approved at the Executive Yuan meeting on the morning of the 21st. The main points are recorded as follows: (1) Regarding the regulations for the Vocational Training Classes for Graduates from Colleges and Above, a draft has been prepared and will be submitted to the Executive Yuan for record. (2) The budget estimate is set at 400,000 yuan, and the budget proposal will be submitted to the Executive Yuan for forwarding to the Central Political Committee for approval. The Ministry of Finance is also requested to advance the funds, starting from September this year, with 40,000 yuan allocated monthly and forwarded by the Executive Yuan. (3) Regarding the method of recruiting students, attention should be paid to ensuring that the schools responsible for guaranteeing students assess whether the students have made any remarks or actions that violate the Three Principles of the People or any other immoral behavior during their time at the school. In addition to the school principal being the natural guarantor, there must be another guarantor with a legitimate occupation and a fixed address. Detailed methods should be specified in the recruitment regulations. (4) The method and standards for reviewing applicants will be formulated after registration. (5) Performance evaluation during the internship period will be conducted by the internship institutions. (6) Preparatory matters will be carried out jointly by representatives from each Standing Committee member, convened by the representative from the Central Political School.

(Central News Agency, Nanjing, July 21st) The Executive Yuan approved the regulations for the Vocational Training Classes for Graduates from Colleges and Above in the morning of the 21st, totaling ten articles. The main points are: (1) The Executive Yuan will establish a Preparatory Committee for the Vocational Training Classes for Graduates from Colleges and Above to handle vocational training matters. (2) Affiliated with the Central Political School. (3) There will be one director, who will be the Director of Education of the Central Political School and a member of the Preparatory Committee, responsible for the training. (4) Students will be recommended by colleges and above for recent three-year graduates (i.e., 1933, 1934, and 1935) who are currently unemployed, and by the Ministry of Education for recent three-year graduates from colleges and above abroad who are currently unemployed. They will be admitted to the training class after being reviewed by the Review Committee and passing the physical examination. (5) The student quota is fixed at 1,000, recruited in one batch, divided by subject, with two training periods, each training period lasting four months, and an internship of three to four months. (6) During the training period, each student will receive a monthly subsidy of 30 yuan (including food, accommodation, and pocket money). During the internship period, each student will receive a subsidy of 40 yuan (including food and accommodation). (7) Students must strictly comply with all orders and rules. (8) Students who pass the evaluation after completing the training and internship will be given a certificate and assigned work according to their performance.

Four Departments Confer on Children's Well-being, Establishing a Permanent Organization 167

The National Committee for Children's Welfare, initiated by the host organization of the National Children's Year Implementation Committee, the three ministries of Interior, Education, and Industry, and the Department of Health, was formed after the conclusion of Children's Year. A draft of "Organizational Regulations for the National Committee for Children's Welfare," consisting of fourteen articles, has been prepared. A discussion meeting was held at the Ministry of Education on the 20th to discuss this draft and other related matters. Present were Wu Shizhong and Chen Lunmin from the Ministry of Interior, Tang Jianfei and Fan Shouzang from the Ministry of Industry, Zhu Zhanggeng and Jin Baoshan from the Department of Health, and Gu Shusen, Lei Zhen (represented by Zheng Yanghe), Wu Yan Yin, and Xue Tianhan from the Ministry of Education, totaling ten people. The meeting was chaired by Wu Yan Yin, and the following decisions were made: (1) After the conclusion of National Children's Year, it was unanimously agreed that there was a need to establish a permanent organization to address the welfare of children nationwide. (2) The draft organizational regulations for the committee should be revised, and the Ministry of Education was requested to revise it and send it to the various departments for review. (3) Regarding children's welfare initiatives, work should begin in the Beijing area, using the remaining funds of over ten thousand yuan from the National Children's Year Implementation Committee over the past year to fund children's welfare projects in Beijing.

Furthermore, regarding the revision of the organizational regulations, those present unanimously advocated for three key points: (1) In terms of organization, the Ministry of Education should be the primary organizing body, with the Ministries of Interior and Industry and the Department of Health playing a participating and jointly organizing role. (2) The committee should have one full-time Secretary-General and several full-time staff members. (3) Expenses should be jointly borne by the three ministries and the department, with extreme frugality in administrative expenses, and the majority of funds should be used for children's welfare projects.

The tasks of this Children's Welfare Committee are fourfold: (1) Promoting children's education; (2) Addressing children's health; (3) Protecting and providing relief for children; (4) Organizing, guiding, and improving children's welfare organizations. Once the three ministries and the department jointly approve the organizational regulations, and each appoints personnel and invites several committee members with expertise and experience in children's welfare, the committee will be formally established.

Zhejiang Province Middle School Graduation Exam - Junior High School Results 169

Physics, Chemistry, and Mathematics are the Best

The results of the second Zhejiang Province Middle School Graduation Examination of the 24th year, for the senior high school section, have been notified to the various schools. The junior high school section has also been verified and announced yesterday. A total of 78 schools, including the Provincial Hangzhou Junior High School, participated in the examination, with 2,608 students taking the exam. Except for the scores of 20 students from Wenlian and 30 students from Yanzhong that have not been received, 2,550 students achieved passing grades in all subjects. 2,168 students were approved for graduation, accounting for over 85% of the total. 348 students who failed one or two subjects were allowed to retake the exam in the next session. 34 students who failed three or more subjects were required to repeat the grade. It is reported that physics, chemistry, and mathematics were the best-performing subjects in both the senior and junior high school examinations.

After the Zhejiang University Agricultural College Abolished the Forestry Department 171

Chinese Forestry Society Strives

After Zhu Kezhen, the president of Zhejiang University, arrived in Xin, he appointed Wu Fuzhen as the dean of the Agricultural College. Dean Wu plans to abolish the Forestry Department starting next semester, as reported in previous newspapers. After this news was released, the Chinese Forestry Society immediately convened an emergency board meeting. It was noted that Zhejiang had established a forestry program for 24 years, with a relatively long history and achievements that were no weaker than other universities. Now that the government is focusing on forests, how could the school abolish the forestry department? Therefore, it was unanimously decided that the Chinese Forestry Society should petition Chairman Chiang and the Ministry of Education to order the university to pay attention to forestry. More than ten people, including Ling Daoyang, Li Yingong, Hui Jikuan, Yao Chuanfa, Pi Zuoqiong, Chen Rong, and Liang Xi, jointly wrote to Dean Wu, requesting that he jointly value forestry.

Municipal Bureau of Education Warns China Wireless Radio Training Institute 175

Unauthorized Use of the Name of Engineering School for Enrollment; Strict Crackdown If Not Corrected

Recently, the Municipal Bureau of Education, due to the China Wireless Radio Engineering Training Institute's failure to comply with bureau orders and unauthorized use of the name "Engineering School" for enrollment in newspaper advertisements, causing confusion among young people, issued a special order to the school, stating that the registered name of the institute in the bureau is the Shanghai Private China Wireless Radio Engineering Training Institute. However, the institute has been using the name "Engineering School" externally. The bureau has previously sent personnel to correct this. However, recent newspaper advertisements for enrollment by the institute still unauthorizedly use the name "Engineering School." This is a blatant violation of bureau orders and causes confusion among young people, which is highly inappropriate. The institute is now given three days from the receipt of this notice to revise the enrollment advertisements. If such incidents occur again in the future, strict punishment will be imposed. Compliance is expected. It is reported that the Municipal Bureau of Education has recently noticed that various supplementary schools, two-session schools, and training institutes in the city frequently fail to comply with the Bureau of Education's regulations and unauthorizedly change the names approved for establishment or registration. Some even use the name "XX Vocational School" in newspaper advertisements. All such cases will be strictly cracked down upon.

Rice and Flour Market Fluctuations: Flour Prices Below August Follow Limited Prices, Plummeting by Six to Seven Cents; Rumors of a Bull Breakup Spreading 179

Yesterday, after the opening of the flour market in the morning, the prices for each month suddenly changed drastically. Except for the current month, which was still similar to the limited price, the remaining months uniformly did not follow the limited price and plummeted. The situation was naturally surprising at first glance, but it was normal in the speculative market. Because the current inventory of each factory is sufficient, selling began with the August contracts. It is rumored that the outside bull group had broken apart. The initial price was still one dime and two cents, but sellers were very active and the price fell continuously. The August price closed at only 3.0825 yuan. The prices for September and later months also uniformly plummeted from the second round, with December being the most severe. The closing price was only one dime and three cents, a drop of eight cents from the fixed limited price, and it seemed to fall by more than one dime compared to the dark market a few days ago. By the time the afternoon market opened, the current month could no longer resist and slightly dropped by half a cent from the limited price. The sentiment for August to November remained poor, and the prices fell another one, two, or three cents. Fortunately, bears actively covered, and prices rebounded slightly. From this, it can be inferred that the market's rise in the past month was mostly driven by speculation. Now that the situation has changed and unexpectedly turned downward, it is a good sign after the previous high prices.

Slight Decline in Wheat Prices 180

Yesterday, the wheat futures market was generally calm after the opening in the morning. Although foreign wheat quotations from Chicago rose by three, four, or five cents, and Canadian quotations rose by four or five cents, the market sentiment was poor because grain merchants, considering the excessively high standards, were actively hedging their physical stocks. This is the environment that should have existed in reality, which the profit-seeking bulls naturally did not expect. Therefore, the market sentiment for each month was flat. By the time the afternoon market opened, the market sentiment for each month remained soft, but the decline was not very large, with a maximum of eight or nine cents. If the rumors of a flour bull breakup are true, the subsequent situation is likely to be repeated. Currently, the wheat market sentiment is stable, and the opening prices for each grade are similar to before: Kai Mingguang Shaheji Guandian Wheat is 4.55 yuan, and Daqiao Wheat is 4.45 yuan. Fuxin handled 5,000 bags, and Shenda and Fufeng handled 1,000 bags each.

More than 20,000 bags arrived in the past few days, and more than 10,000 bags arrived in the past two days. With strong arrivals, it is difficult for the rice market to rise. Fortunately, the current sales of local Ke rice are exceptionally active. If the future supply slightly decreases or the sales volume increases further, the price will also need to rise. American Cotton Spot Prices are Extremely Firm; Futures Prices Rebound as Wall Street Buys; English and Indian Prices Continue to Fall; Three-Grade Yarn and Cotton Also Rise 185

Yesterday, the American cotton market opened with sluggish conditions. The prices for each month fluctuated by 1-2 points, and there were not many sellers. Then, as fellow traders and Liverpool bought, the market price rebounded. Some believe that the bulls have finished closing out their positions, and the market is now entirely dependent on hedging. The current cotton spot prices are extremely firm, and textiles are quiet and soft. Before the close, bull closing and cotton farmer hedging led to renewed weakness. Indian cotton initially fell due to large-scale bull closing and futures traders selling, but later rebounded due to large-scale purchases by European exporters and spot traders. Trading within the exchange was not heavy. Da De Cheng, Fu Xing Yong, Yuan Mao Yong, Qian Chang Xiang, Xiang Feng, Chun Yuan Yong, Wan Xing, Da Fa Yong, and others were on the selling side.

It was found that the market situation for the first half of the day was uncertain and weak. The morning opening was 1132.4 yuan, and the noon closing was 1132.3 yuan. The highest price was 1133 yuan, and the lowest price was 1131.7 yuan, with a fluctuation of 1.3 yuan. As a result, the price fell by 1.6 yuan compared to the previous Saturday. There were 1,911 provisions remaining for this month, with a total of nine long parties and nine short parties. There were 2,849 provisions remaining for August, with a total of fifteen long parties and seventeen short parties. There were 11,067 September contracts, with a total of forty-three long parties and twenty-seven short parties. The total trading volume for the first half of the day was 2,758 provisions.

Exchange Market Trading Mostly Swaps - Results Slightly Tight 187

Yesterday's exchange market transactions were mostly swaps. The process was vague, and the result was slightly tight. Early in the morning, overseas telegrams indicated that London's prime rates should not move in the short term, with forward rates rising by 0.0625. It was said that India sold off after the market closed, and speculators bought in at the posted prices, resulting in a balanced market. New York's silver market remained unchanged. Monte Carlo's forward silver prices remained unchanged, rising by up to 5 hao and falling by up to 2%. London's raw gold fell by 2 pence. The British pound rose against the US dollar by 1.25, the British pound rose against the French franc by 9 pounds sterling, the US dollar fell against the British pound by 0.25, and the US dollar fell against the French franc by 0.25. The Central Bank's posted prices were announced, with the British pound and US dollar both flat. Customs gold units fell by 0.02. The exchange market opened in the morning with the spot selling price of the British pound at 1 shilling 2 and 375/1000 pence, and the US dollar at 30 yuan 125/1000, which was 0.03125 tighter for the British pound and 0.0625 tighter for the US dollar compared to the previous close. After opening, the market slightly hardened. Although foreign firms settled in shillings, banks were all sellers. The Hong Kong and Shanghai Banking Corporation's posted prices were announced, with the British pound and US dollar both flat, and the market hovered. Later, the silver equalization tax was announced unchanged. Banks had mixed opinions. Transactions were mostly swaps. At noon, the general trend hovered. In the afternoon, forward East Asian currencies were bought in and spot currencies were sold out. Banks also traded the British pound and US dollar against each other. The process gradually flattened out, but the general trend was more vague. At the close, the spot selling price of the British pound was 1 shilling 2 and 375/1000 pence, and the US dollar was 30 yuan 125/1000. There were no swaps between the spot and July prices. Compared to the previous close, the British pound was 0.03125 tighter and the US dollar was 0.0625 tighter. In terms of forward prices, the British pound was flat and the US dollar was 0.03125 tighter. Transactions were mostly swaps. The transaction records for today are listed below.

Securities - Government Bonds Mostly Sold in the Afternoon - Large Difference Between Near and Far Terms 188

Yesterday, the Chinese Merchants Securities Exchange experienced a sudden and dramatic change in market conditions. Initially, due to positive sentiment, the long positions were firm, forming a short squeeze. Market prices rose sharply, with Class A bonds for the current month breaking through to a new high price of 69 yuan 2 jiao, reaching 69 yuan 7 jiao. Because many short positions were swaps, the forward market prices were inverted in each round. Subsequently, rumors of instability emerged during the day, and the long positions exited, causing a large drop. Market conditions changed rapidly. High market prices are particularly prone to unexpected declines. Due to the approaching settlement, it is said that the Sichuan bankers have temporarily stopped using legal tender, and may also exit the market. Yesterday's process began with extremely high morale. Everyone believed that the environment was peaceful, and many remained firm and unmoved. The short positions panicked again, hedging or swapping positions one by one. Therefore, the recent surge was particularly strong. Except for numbers 4, 35, and 48, most buyers were retail investors. The market price improved by 2-3 jiao to 8.5 jiao. Class A bonds for the current month reached a new high price. The forward market was less strong, with each item showing inverted prices. In the first round of the afternoon auction, morale remained firm. Types E and D rose by another 1.5 to 4.5 jiao. When auctioning Type C, number 4 suddenly changed its style and tended to sell. Those who followed included numbers 11, 14, and later 13 and 47, etc., all selling one after another. Type C was suppressed by number 4, and the forward market turned down by 3.5 jiao. The Type B forward market even fell by as much as 7 jiao. Type A also fell by more than half a yuan. Market sentiment changed very quickly. The trend was that the continuous short squeeze may turn into a long squeeze. As a result, market prices varied greatly. The Type B forward market fell by 1 jiao, while the Type D spot market rose by 1 yuan and 5 fen. The rest mostly improved, rising by 1.35 jiao to 6.8 jiao. The total volume of transactions was 11.127 million yuan. The resulting increases and decreases are compared in the table on the left. (Unit: yuan, transaction unit: 100 yuan)

Piece Goods - Dasheng Flannelette Futures Have Been Sold - Fine Cloth, Fine Twill, Yangtze and Cantonese Merchants Are Buying Heavily 189

Yesterday, the price of raw yarn for the near month was falling. However, the cloth market was able to maintain its position due to thin inventory. Sentiment has already seen downstream effects, and sales of all goods were very stable. East Asian fine cloth, fine twill, and market cloth also showed a recovery of 2.5 fen per piece. The market for fine cloth and fine twill from this factory was quite strong due to the strong demand from the Yangtze and Cantonese merchants. Yesterday, the Cantonese merchants bought more than 500 pieces of fine twill for next month's futures for each brand, as well as more than 30 boxes of straight tribute, serge, crepe, etc. spot goods. The Changsha merchants bought more than 200 pieces of fine cloth and fine twill from this factory. More than 100 boxes of printed straight tribute serge and printed cloth, etc., from factories such as Lun Chang. The Sichuan merchants bought more than 100 pieces of Lun Chang's "Heroic Figure" blue cloth, Dacheng blue cloth, etc., as well as 70-80 pieces of serge, straight tribute, crepe, etc. Sales were also seen in Wuhu. Yesterday, more than 100 pieces of fine cloth, fine twill, and serge were sold. Dasheng Factory's 16-pound, 13-pound, and 9-pound flannelette futures were opened for sale yesterday, with more purchases from wholesale shops on this street and merchants from the Yangtze and Shandong regions. Zhen Tai Factory's 14.5-pound "Hongfu" flannelette, and Yihua Factory's "Three Peaches Three Deer" bleached flannelette, also had futures opened for sale. The wholesale shops on this street had the strongest demand.

Rice-Colored Fat Leather Unexpectedly Refreshed Again 190

Yesterday, transactions in wool were almost non-existent. The prices of goods did not fluctuate significantly. However, old fat leather in rough rice yellow color has been selling exceptionally well recently, showing signs of a renewed interest from tailors. As a result, the market price suddenly rose by 2-3 jiao. In addition, there is a shortage of goods in the market, and new goods are very scarce this summer. As a result, after a day of popularity, they were almost completely collected. There is a shortage and prices have soared. Fat leather that was initially sold for 2 yuan and 4 jiao per yard is now selling for 2 yuan and 7.5 jiao. Rice-colored ones require an additional 1 jiao. Those in the trade who have stock are quite regretful that they lack it.

Silk and Tea - Yokohama Futures and Spot Silk Both Fall More Than 10 Yuan 191

Yesterday, the Yokohama silk market continued to decline. Spot sales opened 12.5 yuan lower than the previous day, and futures fell 15 yuan. In the Lyon silk market, Shanghai's AB grades both held their original prices, and Japanese silk also remained unchanged. New York Standard Silk's spot and futures opened slightly higher by 0.5 to 1 fen. The remaining Japanese and Chinese silk products did not change. The Shanghai market was quite sluggish, and sentiment was softening. Yesterday, only Lian Na and users had some demand.

Fine Eyebrow Green Tea Sales Slightly Slow 193

Yesterday, the green tea market was slightly quiet. European firms have all taken a wait-and-see attitude due to the recent outbreak of war in Morocco. Yesterday, a total of more than 970 boxes of black and green tea were traded. Sales of fine eyebrows saw a decrease of 3-4 yuan. Sales of needle eyebrows saw a decrease of 1-2 yuan. Transactions in Qi Duo black tea were particularly slow. However, British and Russian firms have shipped no less than 5,000 boxes of black tea, flower tea, and other goods in recent days, which is quite strong compared to before.

According to a report from the Tea Industry Association, transactions in fine eyebrows from various regions were still not numerous yesterday. However, Tianyu bought a total of more than 400 boxes of fine eyebrows from Yushan and local merchants. Mid-grade Tun Wu fine eyebrows were 75-76 yuan, and high-grade were more than 80 yuan. Yihua Jinlong and other firms had sporadic transactions. Bai Tou firm was still able to offer 104 yuan for high-grade Wu Zhen, but the goods were quite rare. Transactions in needle eyebrows priced at 30-40 yuan were considered quite good. It is said that the Gui Xi Wen Xie Association also intends to start buying, so the future is still optimistic. Due to mismatched prices offered by foreign firms, large merchants of Pingshui tea have not been able to transact this week, with only Gai Lu Zhen Mei Xiehe purchasing about 200 pieces at a price of 31 yuan to 33 yuan.

Metals Westhay Iron Price Soars 196

Westhay iron is selling well in this port. A considerable amount has been offered on the market, and standard asking prices are rising steadily due to insufficient supply. The current market price is 33 yuan per box. Large boxes of thin gauge iron can fetch as much as 34.5 yuan per box. Yesterday's market saw transactions of 400 to 500 boxes, but inventories are remarkably low, boosting confidence. Moreover, overseas prices soared to 8 gold yuan yesterday, an increase of 4 gold jiao from the previous level, further encouraging holders to hold onto their goods.

Spring and Autumn

Anecdotes 197

— (Ming Ran)

Human Behavior One can compare the Abyssinia to the sheep, Italy to the tiger, and England and France to the fox! The cicada and the weaver bird can be compared to China, the tirelessly working ant can be compared to Germany, the American dollar diplomacy can be compared to the praying mantis... Perhaps one can think of another country, but what about the snake!

In the summer, men and women who are good at swimming can be compared to the amphibious frog—blood-sucking mosquitoes can be compared to usurers, flies that disturb the peace can be compared to vagrants—

People pursuing urban careers, whether they are graduates or unemployed students, can be compared to bees and butterflies!

The hardworking farmers in the fields can be compared to the water buffalo dragging the plow—traitorous and depraved collaborators, self-inflicted harm, can be compared to moths flying towards the fire at night. People who enlighten and guide society can be compared to fireflies flashing their lights in the summer night, preventing people from getting lost and wandering astray!

On Mosquitoes 198

— Chen Liang

Some old fellows who like to talk about the current situation often compare the current situation to malaria, and from malaria, they talk about the scourge left by mosquitoes, and advocate wiping out mosquitoes, which is already more than half the way to thinking about the problem. Now, my discussion of mosquitoes is of a different nature.

In fact, mosquitoes use their stingers to bite people, but they don't always cause malaria. According to the analysis of pathology, there are two kinds of mosquitoes, one is the common mosquito, with the Western name Culex, and the other is the malaria mosquito, with the Western name Anopheles. In our vulgar eyes, we only know that the buzzing flying creatures are mosquitoes. They are extremely evil, and should be killed without mercy. We will never let them bite on our skin and then study them carefully. But since the Western devils have taken the trouble to identify them, our compatriots, for the sake of fun, may as well be happy to know some readily available information.

With a little attention, they can be distinguished, because when malaria mosquitoes perch on a wall, their heads face the wall and their tails face outward, in a diagonal position. When common mosquitoes perch on a wall, their heads and tails hang straight down, parallel to the wall. The wings of malaria mosquitoes have patterns and spots, and their bodies form a straight line from the proboscis to the tail. The wings of common mosquitoes are transparent, with patterns but no spots, and the shape of the body, head, and chest is bent, forming an obtuse angle with the abdomen. When it comes to the movements of malaria mosquitoes, they only appear in the dark at night, taking advantage of the fact that people cannot see them or are asleep, to plunder blood and fatten themselves. They fly very low, with a ghostly air. They are sinister and perverse, making people afraid. They not only plunder people's nourishing elements, but also transmit a kind of malaria protozoa, MallaliaePlaxmodium, into human blood, destroying the tissue of blood cells, which is as hateful as troublemakers disrupting order. As for common mosquitoes, although they also suck human blood, their attitude is better and does not cause great disasters.

If we are to judge and punish according to the crime, we will of course only punish malaria mosquitoes.

However, Chinese compatriots mostly harbor a kind of "virtue of loving life," walking with their heads down to avoid trampling ants to death, so they let the mosquito larvae in stagnant water grow and change naturally. When they themselves are bitten painfully, they slap them to death, thinking that it is a karmic retribution. If they do not die and fly away, they think that the mosquito's life should not be cut short. However, Westerners have a stubborn prejudice, advocating "killing all mosquitoes." Smart people think to themselves: isn't this still the stupid thing of "the Foolish Old Man Removing the Mountain"?

University Student's Home 199

— Hua Ling

In a lane of twelve shikumen (stone gate) houses, the most eye-catching is the university student's home, which is in the last two-story house. In the lane, when this shikumen is mentioned, people never say someone's surname or mansion, but always say "the university student's home."

The university student's father is a speculative businessman. The university student is his father's only son. His father has been quite successful in speculation for many years. Originally, nine families lived together in the two-story house. Since he made a fortune four years ago, he drove away the other eight tenant families and lived there alone. Once poor people have money, everything is different. They don't care much about their neighbors. At that time, the university student had just graduated from middle school. His father had money anyway, so he decided to send him to a certain university. The neighbors, seeing that his family gradually broke off contact with the surrounding neighbors, became too lazy to say someone's surname, and then called it "the university student's home."

Speaking of this university student's home, it really made the neighbors in the other eleven shikumen houses half envious and half jealous. In the two-story house, there lived only the university student's parents and the university student himself, but they employed five people, including a rickshaw puller, a nanny, and a maid. These servants also ate big fish and meat every day. What did the master eat? Naturally, it goes without saying. In short, the superiority of their life was something that no family in the entire lane could hope to achieve even half of.

Three years passed quickly. In a speculative market storm, the university student's father gambled again and again, not only losing everything but also incurring a lot of debt that could not be repaid, and went bankrupt. A notice of seizure was pasted on the door. The family took a few blankets and temporarily took refuge in a pavilion in House No. 8. To make matters worse, the university student's father became ill from anger and anxiety and died. After a hasty funeral, the mother and son faced each other with furrowed brows, at a loss. The university student was no longer as carefree as before. After living there for three months, the university student could not find a job, and the mother and son returned to their hometown alone and forlorn.

However, in a shikumen at the end of that lane, even though another family now lives there, the people in the lane still call it "the university student's home."

Germs 200

— Jin Shan

One person was about to eat food that flies had landed on, and another person advised him, "Don't eat that food, I'm afraid it has microorganisms on it!" The fool said, "You say there are microorganisms, why can't my eyes see them?"

The above story is really a joke. The morphology of germs is extremely small, and it is definitely not something that human eyes can see. Only when viewed under a microscope with staining can the dots and curves be clearly presented before our eyes. But precisely because it is a minute object that cannot be observed by oneself, people often suffer its harm in carelessness.

There are many kinds of microorganisms. Just talking about infectious bacteria, there are dozens of kinds. For example, "tubercle bacillus" will cause tuberculosis, "cholera vibrio" will cause cholera, "meningococcal coccus" will cause meningitis, etc. According to the investigation of the Health Work Department, these infectious bacteria kill tens of millions of people every year!

However, although the harm of infection is severe, the effect of prevention is also great. In recent years, domestically produced bactericidal agents include "Yalin Zishui" and "Yalin Shaer" (produced by Wuzhou Pharmacy), one specifically for watering walls and corners to eliminate places where microorganisms accumulate, and one specifically for bathing and washing to prevent indirect transmission of bacterial toxins. This can also be said to be a formidable enemy of microorganisms.

Thoughts on the Reprint of Imperial Incense Drifting Record 201

— Qin Shouou

A reprint is just a reprint, what is there to feel or not feel?

In fact, it is something that every person engaged in writing cannot help but have! Because when we write a book, it is really like giving birth to a son, and it is both father and mother, taking on both roles, making it even more laborious than giving birth to a son. When it is completed and published, we have even more expectations and hopes for it. Fortunately, it is praised by some people and actually gets reprinted. Tell me, how can we not have some feelings?

This time it's my turn! Although my works have been reprinted more than just this Imperial Incense Drifting Record, the situation this time is a bit different: first, because the market is still sluggish, especially in the publishing industry, and Imperial Incense Drifting Record can be reprinted immediately after the first edition in two months, it can be said to be a very rare thing; second, the structure and style of this book are very special, both the original and the translation are like this. Whether this special flavor is suitable for modern readers, I had absolutely no confidence at the beginning. Now, although I dare not say it has been successful, it has not been a complete failure. It is indeed a bit lucky to have this result after the first attempt. So when Mr. Ma Yinliang, the manager of Shenbao, notified me that it would be reprinted immediately, I really had a mix of surprise and joy in my heart.

I was surprised because the content of this book is really not very perfect, and the translation is especially mediocre. If it is spread indefinitely, it will really lead to "good things don't go out the door, but bad things travel a thousand miles!" I was happy because I like this kind of novel very much, and others don't seem to hate it. It's just that I'm still planning to continue to introduce one or two works by Deling, and this will increase my courage a bit.

Swapping the Nest with the Luan Phoenix 202

— Written by Zhang Henshui

Chapter 4: Sight and Hearing Are Not Floating Dust, Reassuring Reply Sent, Life and Death Can Be Generous, Expressing Sadness in Poetry

He bowed deeply to his mother and said, "Please rest assured, Mother, I will definitely not delay my studies." After saying this, he took his textbooks and hurried out. As he was leaving, he heard his mother tell the maid Zhou, "I knew he was very anxious, afraid of delaying his studies. But he was afraid of making me anxious, so he didn't say a word. Later, the meal should be earlier, don't let him worry." Guoshi listened, and a kind of gratitude he couldn't express came over him. He thought that his pursuit of a young lady was something his mother didn't expect. It's good that Jiang Mailan rejected my request, so that I wouldn't be so distraught. With this thought, he didn't go around the bend to meet Miss Jiang, but took the direct road to school. If he couldn't get her reply, then there was no need to wait for her reply. In this way, he cooled down his thoughts for more than a day. When he came back for lunch that day, he saw a letter on his desk. The letter had his name on it, and the postscript said "details inside." Seeing the beautiful handwriting, it was clearly a woman's handwriting. Before he even opened the letter, his heart was already pounding. So he slowly took the letter in his hand, first sat down on the chair, and calmed himself down. Then he opened the letter. It was just an ordinary eight-line letter, which read:

To Mr. Litian's esteemed seat: Having read your letter, Mother and I are frightened. Lan guards herself like jade, and rarely associates with others. Although she often reads great articles and admires you as a contemporary author, there are many suspicions, and she dare not regard you as a close friend. Moreover, our family rules are strict, and we adhere to the style of books. In the remaining years of hardship, I only have the pain of many difficulties. These twists and turns cannot be fully explained in a single letter. I hope you, a gentleman, will cherish yourself and not implicate others in sin. I am very fortunate. My tender heart is turning a hundred times, and I cannot complete the writing. I send this reply specially, and wish you well. Jiang Menglan bows again.

In these eight lines, there was also more than one line of blank space, with a small line added above, please do not send any more letters. At first glance, he felt that he had been rejected by someone. (51)

Local Customs and Minor Chronicles

The Internationally Mysterious Yokohama 203

— Ji Yun

From our country to Japan, the first port is either Nagasaki or Yokohama. The most overseas Chinese from our country live in Yokohama, so the relationship with our country is the deepest. Moreover, European and American ships all use Yokohama as the docking port for Japan, and people from all countries who pass through Japan must disembark in Yokohama once to listen to and appreciate some oriental interests, so Yokohama has become an international port since its opening, until now. It is said that when the envoy from our country went to Japan, he also brought guards and attendants, advancing with the same shouts and clearing the way as in his own country, and the Japanese had to avoid and disperse. The difference from the current situation is like heaven and earth. Even with unequal treaties, Japan has also concluded many. To this day, there are still leased lands of various countries such as Britain and France in Yokohama City that have not been recovered. Although they are not like the concessions in our country, they occupy them without paying taxes.

When foreign ships dock in Yokohama, foreigners mostly go ashore to visit and buy some things. The nearby Japanese vendors often transport goods and peddle them on the ships, and the decks and corridors become their temporary shops. The goods are mostly daily necessities, rayon silk, and toys. The shops on the streets also rely on foreign customers as their only patrons, so the goods in Yokohama City are transformed by the psychology of foreigners. The most numerous are antique shops, postal shipping companies, and international exchange shops. There are also more rickshaws than in Tokyo, and foreigners often sit on the cars with their long legs to play. They don't want to use it as a means of transportation, but to try oriental tastes.

Yokohama's night is mysterious. There are countless exotic hotels in the city, all maintained by foreigners. After foreigners go ashore, most of them are unwilling to return to the ship, so they stay overnight in hotels. The boredom of long-distance travelers can be eliminated in dance halls and hotels. Prostitution and secret occupations are very developed in Yokohama City. Dacaoying is full of dance halls, cafes, and hotels. These women can all speak fluent foreign languages, including English, French, German, and Russian. Many of them are veterans who have been to Shanghai and Paris and have experienced the world, and they are very skilled in dealing with foreigners. Last year, it was reported that a foreign professor at a university in Tokyo was filming a pornographic movie in Yokohama, which was a leak of a wisp of spring light.

Since there are so many foreigners staying in Yokohama, the nationalities and races are extremely complicated. Unscrupulous foreigners are also learning to do mysterious business. Tokyoites who like mystery all rush there by car and train. The gambling dens, brothels, and hotels are all better than in Tokyo. Yokohama seems to be another world, indeed a mysterious international port. Otherwise, why can things that are not available in other places be openly available in Yokohama? Recently, three beautiful foreigners were discovered who dress up like women all day long and go in and out of the revolving halls, not to mention another pornographic incident.

The overseas Chinese in Yokohama are all honest merchants. Nanjing Street is full of Chinese restaurants. The cabinets are full of wine pots, warm pots, shark fins, and dried scallops. Foreign tourists and Japanese people like them very much. And in the grocery stores, even my old-fashioned palace powder and sacrificial tin foil are available, truly all-encompassing. These pure merchants, who do not enter the mysterious vortex, are very admirable.

The Words of a Back Scrubber 204

— Among them

Every time I go into the bathhouse to wash up, the back scrubbers always run up to me with twelve points of hope; but because I don't need it, they finally retreat with eleven points of disappointment. Recently, because I accidentally burned my hand on an alcohol lamp, I went into the bathhouse, and the back scrubber came over, so I didn't let him be disappointed again.

While the back scrubber was scrubbing my back, he chatted with me, so I asked about their living conditions. Now, I will record a passage of the back scrubber's conversation as follows.

"Sir: this bowl of rice of ours is really not profitable. It seems that we get a dime for scrubbing a customer's back, but in fact we only get four cents, and the boss takes six cents. There are more than a dozen back scrubbers in the bathhouse. On average, each person does more than ten businesses a day, which is extremely good, so at most we can only get half a yuan a day. Some people have no choice and secretly tell the customers to give the dime directly to the back scrubber. If the boss knows about this, the rice bowl will be broken immediately. So careful people dare not. Furthermore, business is not as good as it used to be. The biggest reason is that there are too many massage parlors and co-ed baths. There are almost massage places on every street. They also shout big prices for competition, such as bathing, back scrubbing, and beautiful women for only half a yuan. You think, going to the bathhouse, the most exquisite thing is to spend half a yuan, and now they only have half a yuan, everyone is willing to go there! Because no man doesn't like women touching him all over, and our business has been taken away by the massage parlors. Alas, now it's really a woman's world, women have all the advantages!"

Shen Bao Local Supplement

Commentary

Japanese Military Exercises and the Order to Study the Classics 213

— Xiang

In the Shen Bao of the 19th, the following two news items that echoed each other appeared in the same place: One was a report that the Japanese army in Tianjin would conduct large-scale exercises at Nanda Temple for five days starting on the 19th. "160 Japanese cavalrymen, 4 cannons, and 160 horses arrived at Nanda Temple by special train. At 9 o'clock, another 180 infantrymen, with 6 machine guns and 3 heavy military vehicles, also arrived at Nanda Temple on the 41st express train." The other was a report that "the Jizheng Council issued a notice to the two provinces and cities of Ji, Cha, Ping, and Tianjin, ordering all primary and secondary schools to add the study of classics," which is expected to be implemented when school starts next semester. These two news items published together are actually a perfect satirical picture.

The issue of "studying the classics" has been going on for a long time in China. In the past, when Tianjin was in a critical situation, we saw in the newspapers that the Jizheng Council ordered all civil servants in Pingjin to study the "Four Books and Five Classics" outside of office hours. The meaning of this story need not be explained further. It is truly a case of "Sima Zhao's heart is known to all." Now the Jizheng Council is doing this "elegant" thing again. When we see it, we feel an unusual stimulation on our nerves.

At the same time, in the same place, on one side, tanks and cannons are conducting large-scale military exercises on our land, while on the other side, people who are too "relaxed" are calmly and attentively chanting "poetry says, Confucius says." This is a rare comedic farce in ancient and modern times, but it is also a heartbreaking tragedy. Not long ago, Xiao Zhenying, who held an important position in North China, held a large-scale birthday celebration for his father. The traffic was heavy, making it the first grand event since the "Beijing government." For a time, the commercial market in Pingjin was lively, and there was a sense of "peace and prosperity," as if the world was at peace. An ancient poem says, "The merchant girl does not know the hatred of a fallen country, and still sings 'Backyard Flowers' across the river," which can be compared to the situation at that time. Now the Jizheng Council's order for Pingjin schools to study the classics is in the same vein. We really cannot but thank Xiao Zhenying and his generation for their painstaking efforts to help the people of Pingjin forget the greatest pain they are currently suffering and live in peace and contentment.

However, the current pain, although we can try our best to forget it, but reality is most likely to play tricks on people, and it will give you a greater stimulation from time to time. What will happen then?

School is on Holiday 214

— Laoxin

School is on holiday. The semester exams are over.

Obligatory teacher Xiao Chen is as busy as Sun Wukong, wishing he could have three heads and six arms out of thin air. His responsibility is the full authority of the academic affairs office. The scores of more than 200 students have to drain his dry brain, and there are also the orders issued by the school's "three giants": In order to ensure the increase in the number of students in the next semester, quickly organize a "student achievement exhibition" and prepare a "fun fair" to connect with the parents of the students and communicate feelings. So—— and so on, by order. Our Mr. Xiao Chen is even busier. He jumps around all day, from the school office to the classroom, and from the classroom back to the place where he sleeps—— to put it beautifully, it is: the teachers' dormitory. In that dormitory, which does not see the sun all day and is not much better than a dungeon, he flips through the reference materials he has accumulated over the years, preparing for all this, all this.

The school office has become a market. The students' small heads are constantly rising and falling, and dozens of pairs of small eyes are eagerly and greedily staring at the place where the scorebooks are hung. Perhaps in their little hearts, they are jumping, anxiously and fearfully wanting to know their grades in the shortest possible time—— pass, or fail. Mr. Xiao Chen's head is a little dizzy, and his eyes are a little blurry. Seeing this pile of small heads, he feels like the waves in the sea—— no, to be more precise, it is the small watermelon that he often longs for that can quench his boredom and thirst! So, without paying attention, his hands and brain become uncoordinated, and the beads on the abacus do not listen to his command! Wrong. Enduring his temper, he has to catch up again. The calendar on the desk opened its mouth and smiled mockingly at him—— for two meals a day and a place to sleep at night, he sold himself out like this. —— Damn it, hurry up, tomorrow, tomorrow……

"Tomorrow?"

He was startled. —— Tomorrow is parents' day. The meeting will start at 2 pm, and by that time he will have to finish all the scores, and—— the fun fair; the singing program prepared for the students; the scene "Autumn Sun" directed by friend Zhou; singing performances; costume speeches; ventriloquism; one-man show…… Also, the students' grades; drawings, handicrafts, compositions, and questions and answers for each subject.

His brain became confused. Recently, his neurasthenia has brought him a bad temper. He also thought—— is it really for two meals a day and a place to sleep at night that he has sold all his time? Look——

The principal's lover, a middle-level class teacher, with a strangely ugly face, is playing the piano and singing—— "Good baby, special… fast, ya ya ya ya……"

What a nauseating lewd tune. There is also a group of teachers—— all relatives of the emperor, they (with a her) are joking and laughing softly. If they were seen by the new school of lyricists, they would inevitably praise—— "School affairs, who cares!"

As for the principal and the imposing director of general affairs, they are quite energetic, but the place where they put their energy is different from Xiao Chen. They try their best to win over, or even bribe, the students, decorate the exterior of the school, and plan—— to enroll 400 students next semester, 12 oceans per person, 4 times 4 equals 4, 4 times 2 equals 8, 4,800, how comfortable. However——

"I, Xiao Chen, am busy from morning to night, for two meals a day and a place to sleep at night. Damn it, fuck your ancestors for eighteen generations!……"

Sometimes, Mr. Xiao Chen really wants to give up all this, although the demon of life often shows him a hideous face. However, when his eyes fall on the apple-like faces of these children, his anxiety slows down, and his resentment disappears. He often says to himself—— for them, sacrifice yourself.

He cheered up again to calculate the scores. A large pile of apple-like faces slipped through his eyes. They and she, thanks to him and his two friends' efforts in the past few months, have emerged from the money hole of the merchants, and are lively jumping and calling under the sunlight of nature. Although—— he, Xiao Chen, and those two friends are living in a life without sunlight all day long.

"Mr. Chen, come! Watch our last rehearsal and see if the arrangement is familiar?"

So, he dropped his work again and came to the library to watch them rehearse. When he saw them performing the solemn scene where the father sadly shot his little traitor son, he was also moved. He patted their small shoulders:

"You are working hard! Ask Mr. Zhou to arrange a few more plays for you next semester."

"Mr. Chen," a very weak voice asked Mr. Xiao Chen in a low voice: "I heard that you will not be teaching here next semester, is that true?"

The sudden question shocked Mr. Xiao Chen. He knew about this small disturbance himself. Everything in front of him was dark, he seemed to see that the little achievements of his efforts over the past few months had turned into soap bubbles, and soon it would be blown away by the harsh environment, and he shed a few tears. He raised his legs and walked out of the library, and he heard the buzzing crying behind him.

Lotus 215

— Liao Chuxiu

I have wanted to write an article about lotus flowers for a long time, but I finally haven't written it. I even told a friend about this idea in advance, so when he jokingly said, "The lotus flowers are about to wither," I was really ashamed.

I'm afraid the earliest flowers I saw were lotus flowers. In the yard of our house, I don't know when, there were four neat lotus tanks. Every summer, more than a dozen flowers would bloom, both red and white. Although I was very tired, I didn't see fat lotus flowers when I was a child, so I was always very happy.

In fact, lotus flowers are not beautiful. Their only advantage is "big". Planted in a tank, they are messy and uneven, and the "composition" between the flowers and leaves is really not good, not to mention that there are countless red mosquito larvae swimming in the lush water above the mud. But the reason why I finally like lotus flowers is of course ridiculous to say, but there is no way. I like lotus flowers because their petals can be coated with flour and fried; so as soon as the lotus flowers in the yard bloom, I will immediately artificially scatter them.

I really understood the benefits of lotus flowers when I was sixteen years old. There was a garden near our school. The garden was almost abandoned. The grass grew very high in summer. As soon as we entered, we heard the sound of insects singing in the grass. After walking a few more steps, a large pond lay across our path; this pond was more than ten feet wide and about half a mile long, so a slight breeze could already cause some ripples. On both sides of the pond, there was a row of tall willows, and there were no other miscellaneous trees, which shows that the owner was very extraordinary at the time. A small bridge with railings lay flat on the water. The color of the bridge had already turned gray and black. At the time, I thought it was probably vermilion. Near the bridge surface of the pool, there were a few sparse floating locust leaves, and a little further away, there were some lotus leaves. If we looked further into the distance, a quarter of a mile of the water surface was completely occupied by lotus flowers, and there must have been at least two or three thousand flowers. They were all pink, and bursts of fragrance came in waves, making people feel drunk. Near the bridge, there were also one or two lonely blooms, and the shadows of the clouds and the light of the waves made them look more clear and beautiful. At this time, I began to understand the beauty of the word "graceful" to describe the lotus flower, and then the summer vacation began.

It was autumn, and the cicadas in the tall willows dragged their intermittent remnants. I took the heart of the old tour and went to visit this pond of lotus flowers again. It was really "without seeing the garden, how can you feel the autumn light is so much?" (Forgive me for learning a sentence from Miss Du Liniang's "Returning Soul Record") As soon as I entered the garden gate, I felt that the shade of the tall willows had thinned a lot, and there were already fallen leaves of paulownia on the pebble path. Suddenly I walked up the small bridge and looked forward. At that time, almost all of the two or three thousand lotus flowers had fallen. In the middle of the continuous green canopy, there were only dozens of lotus seedpods, still with one or two petals of residual flowers that had not been taken off, but the tantalizing light red had turned into a pitiful pale white. At this time, I suddenly thought of the two lines of words by Li Yu, the lord of the Southern Tang Dynasty, "The fragrance of the lotus seed pod disappears, the green leaves remain, and the four winds cause sorrow between the green waves." The breeze is still rippling on the water, one is still adding beauty, and now it is "intentionally creating sorrow." Mr. Wang Jing'an explained that these two lines of words mean "all the flowers are dirty, and the beauty is late in life." If you haven't seen the above

Page 20

The realm is not known.

I haven't seen that pond of lotus flowers for eight or nine years, and I haven't even seen the potted lotus flowers in the yard for three or four years. The letter I received from home said that the potted lotus flowers in the yard had long since stopped blooming, and only grew a few thin and pitiful leaves every year. And that lotus pond, probably, was abandoned along with that garden; only those few willow trees must have grown taller.

Peace Tax 216

— Zhifu

May 20th, the birthday of the Dragon King, according to custom, a water dragon is performed on this day, and the streets are more lively than usual.

Sanli Temple—that quiet rural town. Today, I don't know who started it, the sound of gongs woke people from their dreams early in the morning. The whole town was noisy, and even a wild dog would jump up crazily.

In the west of the town, in the open space near the Dragon King Temple, two water dragons, so brilliantly arranged and neat, were surrounded by a large group of dark-skinned men, and the situation seemed very tense and serious.

A Gui is a middle-aged warrior, tall, and has innate superhuman strength. Because of this, he has gained some prestige in the town. In the past, during the Dragon performance season, he would act as a gunman (1), always taking the lead, carrying the heavy spearhead on his shoulder, taking big strides, from this side to that side, blowing a loud whistle, personally leading that very rude crowd, and directing their movements, just like bravely killing the enemy in battle.

Because of this, he gained public admiration, and the annual peace tax (2) was gradually taken over by him alone. Each time, tens of thousands of large coins could be rolled into his pocket without hesitation, and he regarded the Dragon King Festival as a patented business.

This year, A Gui did not give up his right and continued to be the initiator.

But the years have been barren! Since the sound of the gong in the morning, he has routinely carried a rattan basket door-to-door to collect donations. Nine out of ten households are like this; he has to repeat thousands of times to satisfy his desires.

Indeed, the years are getting worse and worse! But who would have thought that it would affect the "peace tax" he controls...?

"A Gui! We always donate 880 cash, this year... this year we can only rely on Grandpa Dragon King... 550... we..." That was Mao, the shopkeeper of the distillery, pushing back at A Gui:

"Uncle Mao! A Gui has the most refreshing temper, here! 770... it's considered a share for the brothers!" With a peaceful smile, A Gui argued with him:

"660!"

"Promotion..."

"We have to wait until next year! If the years are good next year... we'll make up for it... ha, how about that!"

A Gui no longer asked for an increase, entered it in the donation book, waved his hand and stepped into the door of the food store—a more deserted and quiet shop.

The shopkeeper, Zhu Hushizi, was meticulously sweeping up rice crumbs and wheat husks.

"I'm bothering you, this year is peaceful and prosperous... I hope Grandpa will bring in more goods and make more money..." A Gui flattered:

"300 coins... please enter it in the book!" Zhu Hushizi twisted his face, showing a bitter smile, glanced at him, and handed over a pile of copper coins that had turned clear yellow.

"Please promote!... Grandpa."

"This is already the price of a liter of rice!..." He stared resentfully, his eyes looking at the rice grains in the basket, his voice as low and hoarse as a mosquito:

A Gui was moved by that hoarse voice! He also stared blankly at the rice in the granary, and it took him a long time to recover. Once a year! Grandpa... Alright.

"Barren year..." the boss finally spoke sadly, followed by a heavy hum:

They looked at each other... barren year... a liter of rice... peace tax... in the two brains, the same thing was repeated countless times.

A Gui could only slip out of the shop lightly——

Similarly, after donating dozens of households, the weight of the rattan basket still did not increase, and A Gui was too bored; he recalled the convenience of donating in previous years, only this year, it was barren!

His heart was depressed, and his steps became slow and seemed to be shackled, so heavy and sour. The sound of gongs in the distance was still shaking.

When passing through a quiet and deep alley, A Gui cursed heavily! —— Cursing that "barren year": "Fuck her mother!... Grandpa Heaven." Note (1) Gunman The old-fashioned water dragon is equipped with a water gun, and the person who points the gun is called——the gunman.

(2) Peace Tax Each household pays the tax, which can ensure peace. This donation is given to the people in charge of the water dragon, and it is also regarded as their labor cost when disasters occur. The township is commonly known as "Peace Tax".

Zhou Zhenyu and Another妖傳 [Strange Tale]

Yuan Chang (1120) From 12:45 AM to 1:30 AM

The Grand View Garden scenery is very secluded. One might think it's a small isle of Penglai. The current thatched cottage is elegant. Clearly, the beautiful scenery is hidden in the Red Chamber. It hides unmatched flower-like women. People say they are flower-like, but flowers are still shy. Outside the Xiaoxiang Pavilion, the shadows of 琅玕 bamboo trees. Bitter rain and sour wind fill the autumn. Her father is biased and far away, her mother is partial to the garden. Leaning on the carved railing, she cannot stop her hatred. The gardens are wide. The scenery is secluded. Only the crowds of attendants come and go. She's lazy to comb her hair and wash her face. She fears the stars and moon at dusk are like a hook. Hooking up the ten thousand loads of sorrow in her heart. Sadly, her kind mother passed away first. The lonely girl is left at her maternal family's house. The old matriarch loves her like a precious treasure. The sisters' deep feelings throw themselves into her. Far apart from her father, thousands of miles away. Her dream soul often circles over Yangzhou. She hopes for an imperial edict. She will dance in colorful clothes to repay her filial piety. When will she comfort my lifelong wish? She burns incense and prays day and night. The saddest thing is a matter of concern. The two words "lifelong happiness" are not freely decided. Although a good match may be made in the future. Yet, the matchmaker has not been consulted. This feeling is embarrassing to tell outsiders. She sheds tears in the wind under the moon. Her own obsession, her own planning.

Movie News

Tidbits from Art-China 221

The night before, during the filming of "Little Sisters," Yuan Meiyun accidentally triggered a mechanism in the "Map of Treasures" set, causing her to fall into a tunnel eight feet deep. By the time she was rescued, her face was ashen. Fortunately, she only suffered abrasions to her legs and was not seriously injured.

More than half of "Map of Treasures" has been completed. The crew will depart for Wuxi and the surrounding areas in the coming days to shoot outdoor scenes, and are expected to return in five days.

Bao Tianming has been designing the set for "Guangling Temple" recently, without a break.

"Little Sisters" is expected to be completed in mid-next month, and a special issue is being actively edited and will be published before the premiere of "Little Sisters."

Art-China magazine is very popular with readers. The two special issues that have already been published, "Incarnation Girl" and "The Newlywed Massacre," have both sold out.

Recording engineer Gu Zongyi has recently made major improvements to the recording equipment, so the sounds in "Little Sisters" are clearer than in previous films and have reached a state of perfection.

Fang Peilin's new work, "Mysterious Flower" (tentative title), will soon be completed. It is said to be "a serious theme with a humorous performance," and the story is said to be novel.

Yao Shiquan's cinematography in "Little Sisters" made a huge contribution.

"Map of Treasures" is a thrilling and exciting detective film with humor and seriousness, entertainment and education, starring Wang Yin, Zhou Xuan, Wang Cilong, Guan Hongda, Jiang Xiu, Liang Dusheng, Zhao Manna, and others.

The dog actor, Peili, in "Map of Treasures" performs so "beautifully" that it is worthy of applause.

Xu Qinfang and You Guanren both have excellent performances in "Little Sisters."

The list of successful male actors who were recruited by Art-China will be announced soon.

Playboy 222

Playing at the Great Shanghai

Tidbits from Lianhua 223

Since "The Light of Motherhood," Jin Yan has had many works, but in these works, he has never been seen wearing a beautiful suit or a handsome bow tie. In the recent "Go to Nature," he simply doesn't wear any clothes.

Qin Tong's son, Qin Haiyou, has a round face and smiling eyes. One look at him and you know he's a mischievous child. In "The Lost Lamb," he plays a student teasing the old tutor (played by Hong Jingling), driving the old tutor crazy. That hilarious performance is even more interesting than Qin Guanbao's闹學 [making a scene at school] in "Baolian Lantern."

Bai Lu, who played a maidservant in "Metropolitan Landscape," is still playing a maidservant in "Go to Nature." However, the maidservant in "Go to Nature" is a little more flirtatious and passionate. In the play, Han Langen proposed to her.

"The Lost Lamb" is all-encompassing, with chickens, cats, dogs, cows, sheep, and even two tiny butterflies all giving good performances.

Ge Zuozhi, the protagonist of "The Lost Lamb," likes to paint cow snouts. Entering his bedroom is like visiting an exhibition of cow snout paintings.
